As for economic matters, the Little Entente conference will conduct a comprehensive study on the issue of economic cooperation among Central European countries. Portuguese Ship Rebellion Suppressed: Two Ships Bombed and Heavily Damaged; Rebel Soldiers Imprisoned and to Be Judicially Tried 58

Lisbon: Yesterday, a portion of the sailors on the Portuguese small gunboat "Afonso de Albuquerque" and the destroyer "Dão" rebelled, firing upon the Lisbon fort. Fortunately, the fort returned fire, damaging the two ships, and the rebel soldiers surrendered. Lisbon is now as quiet as ever, but the authorities have declared a state of emergency, restricting the movement of troops in Lisbon, and troops have been stationed at all strategic locations. It is reported that six people were killed and nine injured in the incident. According to a statement issued by the Lisbon authorities, the rebellion has been suppressed, all rebel soldiers have been imprisoned, and it is stated that the people and navy of the entire country condemn the rebels' violence. (Reuters, 8th)

Lisbon: After the naval defense ship "Afonso de Albuquerque" and the destroyer "Dão" suddenly rebelled yesterday morning, they were subdued by government forces. The details are as follows: First, the two ships were anchored in the Tagus River. After the rebellion broke out, they weighed anchor and headed for the mouth of the river. Upon hearing the news, the government forces opened fire from the Doutoride Fort on the north bank and the Almada Fort on the south bank, bombarding them. At that time, the "Afonso de Albuquerque" sailed at full speed, hoping to escape, but the shells rained down, and the bow of the ship was damaged, and it eventually ran aground on the right bank. As for the "Dão", after being hit by a shell, it raised a white flag to indicate its surrender. At that time, people on both sides of the river witnessed the bombardment. (Havas, 9th)

Lisbon: It was learned today that the Almada Fort bombarded the rebel ships, killing five people and injuring eight. All officers and soldiers on the two ships have now been arrested. The Almada Fort apparently knew about the rebellion of the two ships in advance, so it fired upon confirmation. The nearby warships and three submarines did not participate in the operation. The British ship "St. Strathmore" was also nearby and hurriedly sailed out to sea to avoid the bombardment. The "Afonso de Albuquerque" battleship is in danger of sinking today, and a barge has been used to tow it to the shore. The "Dão" has floated again and is being towed to the naval dock for repairs. (National, 8th)

Lisbon: Regarding the gunboat rebellion case, the Council of State held a meeting late last night to discuss follow-up measures. Prime Minister Salazar issued a statement afterwards stating that all officers and sailors of the ships will be stripped of their positions and sent to prison for judicial trial on a regular basis. The officers and junior officers who can prove that they did try to suppress the rebellion will be reinstated, but the captains of the ships will not be forgiven under any circumstances. Military and political figures have declared that this incident was accidental and did not involve other ships. When the forts on both sides of the Tagus River bombarded the rebel ships yesterday, they fired a total of twenty-four shells, eighteen of which hit. (Havas, 9th)

Hungary Expresses Opinions on Revising League of Nations Covenant 59

(Geneva) In accordance with the resolution of the special session of the League of Nations Assembly in July, the League of Nations Secretariat solicited the opinions of the member states of the League of Nations on the issue of revising the Covenant. After the governments of various countries responded separately, Hungarian Foreign Minister Kanya sent a letter to the League of Nations Secretariat today, stating Hungary's opinions on revising the League of Nations Covenant, stating that Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant stipulates that economic and military sanctions may be imposed on countries that violate the Covenant and engage in war, but other articles stipulate that disputes that may arise between member states should be resolved by peaceful means and preventive methods, and that all possible efforts should be made to save the situation that may endanger world peace. These two provisions contradict each other in principle and there is an absolute necessity to adjust them. (Havas, 8th)

Pondering the Traces of Battle at Irún: The Ruins and Collapsed Walls Evoke Melancholy; Captives Used as Hostages All Massacred 65

Andaya Yiyu, Special Correspondent of This Newspaper, having previously visited the Spanish city of Irún to inspect the scars of the civil war, recently returned to the city for a second time. Although the Nationalist authorities made it difficult for travelers to enter and leave, they were unable to prevent him. According to reports, Irún is now filled with ruins and collapsed walls, with only isolated residential areas unaffected. The city is currently garrisoned by approximately one thousand Carlist troops of the Requetés, who wear red berets and are surrounded by the ruins. The foreign troops have now all been moved to the high ground in front of Rentería, from which they are attacking San Sebastián. These troops are no longer visible in Irún, and many have also left. Government aircraft are still flying over the city from time to time, dropping bombs, but because they dare not fly low, they rarely hit their targets. When the Carlist troops in the city hear the sound of the aircraft, they fire machine guns into the air, but to no effect. The artillery fire from both sides is largely a waste of ammunition. According to what the special correspondent of this newspaper saw, only one shell fired by the cruiser "Cervera" hit a 155mm cannon in the city, blowing it to smithereens. However, most of the houses in the city have been destroyed by explosives, and it is feared that it will take several years to restore the city to its former glory. (Havas, 9th)

Before the fall of Irún, the government troops executed members of the Nationalist side who had been detained as hostages. Among those killed were Mados, a former cabinet member during the dictatorship of General Rivera, and Antonia Mora, niece of former Prime Minister Mora. After these people were killed, their bodies were not formally prepared for burial. Other prisoners were hastily buried in large pits. Now that the Nationalist troops have entered the city, they have reburied their fallen comrades. The special correspondent of this newspaper, who was inspecting the area at the time, personally witnessed two Carlist members of the Requetés excavating the mass graves. When they saw the bodies, they pulled them out. The bodies were pale and their eyes were filled with dirt. Relatives identified the bodies, and an officer inquired about the appearance of the deceased to confirm their identities. After each body was exhumed, it was placed in a coffin, but the coffins were too small, so the legs of the deceased had to be bent to fit. The former chief of the Irún police was buried in this way. Because of Mados's large physique, he was buried in blankets instead of a coffin. The situation at the front lines is currently calm. A few women can be seen knitting two kilometers from the front lines. Many of the bridges along the road have been destroyed. When the correspondent of this newspaper traveled to the city by car, he had to drive five kilometers on the railway tracks to enter the city. The homes of the citizens are now full of crucifixes and portraits of the Carlist pretender. This is very different from the situation when the government troops were defending the city. (Havas, 9th)

Sunlight Engine: A Great Invention of Modern Times; Publicly Tested at the World Power Conference 70

(Washington) The Third World Power Conference today tested the sunlight engine, which may be considered a great invention of modern times. The inventor is the famous scientist Dr. Abbot, whose lifetime of research has resulted in the invention. It is claimed that the engine can be used commercially, and that it can be used to generate power in place of coal or oil when these resources become scarce. At the conference, Abbot used sunlight as fuel to power a half-horsepower engine, which is a historic first. He had previously tested a type of sunlight engine many times with excellent results. This is the first time that sunlight has been used to power an engine. The principle is that sunlight from the sky on a clear day strikes the horizontal plane at a right angle. If this sunlight can be fully converted into mechanical work, its power is approximately equal to one horsepower. (National Telegram, 8th)

French Strike Wave Resumes; People Complain About Government; Franco's Position Increasingly Precarious 74

(Paris) The wave of strikes in France seems to be erupting again. In the famous Michelin rubber factory in Clermont-Ferrand, a worker was recently fired by the factory. The workers at the factory, who belong to the socialist Confédération Générale du Travail unitaire, believe that the reason for the dismissal is insufficient and immediately went on strike to protest. This happened yesterday afternoon. This morning, 2,000 workers at the factory who belong to the Catholic labor association, the Confédération Française des Travailleurs Chrétiens, believing that there was no sufficient reason for the strike, marched to the prefect's office at 9:00 AM and occupied it. However, the office continued to operate as usual. The Minister of the Interior, Salengro, immediately went to the area to consult with representatives of both labor and management to find a solution. At 6:00 PM, the strikers belonging to the Confédération Générale du Travail unitaire marched to the prefect's office, attempting to break into the office and drive out the Catholic workers. A conflict broke out with the police surrounding the office, resulting in several injuries. Fortunately, the conflict was not serious. The Catholic workers finally left the office at 9:00 PM. In Marseille, labor and management in the metallurgical industry have not yet signed a work contract. The labor side proposed holding a joint meeting to resolve the differences between the two sides, but this was rejected by management. Therefore, the workers in the industry began a strike today. They claim that the metallurgical workers in Paris went on strike for one hour yesterday to protest the "blockade of the Spanish Republic" by various countries (referring to the ban on arms shipments to Spain). The metallurgical workers in Marseille are now standing on the same front as their colleagues in Paris. (Havas, 8th)

Lille, Northern France: More than 30,000 textile workers in the north of France announced a strike at 11:30 this morning, occupying the factories and demanding wage increases and allowing union representatives to negotiate work contracts with management, in accordance with the mediation measures previously formulated by Labor Minister Lebas. The factory owners believe that the time is not yet ripe for this. There has been no action in the main textile centers, such as Roubaix, Tourcoing, and Armentières. (Havas, 9th)

Marseille: 10,000 unnamed metallurgical workers in this port city have announced a strike and are occupying the factories, refusing to leave. The metallurgical employers' association immediately notified the workers that if they did not leave the factories, they would not be allowed to begin negotiations. The authorities in this port city and the Rhône department have summoned representatives of the striking workers to listen to their opinions and try to find a solution. (Havas, 9th)

(London) Fears that Franco's position is increasingly precarious have caused the selling pressure on the franc that began on Monday to resume today, driving the price down to 76.65. The British Equalization Fund intervened and made strenuous efforts to maintain the price to prevent it from falling further. The French Popular Front is increasingly resentful of the ban on arms shipments to Spain, so the Blum government may be replaced by a government with a nationwide consensus. London now believes that if this happens, the fate of the franc will be decided. Regardless of political changes, the continued increase in the cost of living, such as bread, will reduce the excessive value of the franc. The price of bread in France is already two or three times higher than the world average, and there are now signs that workers will continue to demand wage increases. The recent increase in military spending has made the budget deficit even more severe, which can only be made up by the Banque de France. The failure of the "baby bond" experiment has further proven that the French public is unwilling to buy government bonds. (Reuters, 8th)

Hunan Province's Finances are Difficult; Another Loan of 1.4 Million Taken from Three Banks 81

Changsha Communication: He Haoruo, the director of the Finance Department of Hunan Province, has been in office for exactly one year since taking over last year. When he took over, although He had a firm determination to reorganize the finances, Zhang Kailian had left behind debts of more than 3.9 million yuan to various banks and money houses. The monthly interest rate was an average of about 1.3 percent, and even if the principal was not repaid, interest of more than 20,000 yuan had to be paid each month. In addition, the administrative expenses of Hunan Province had accumulated too much over the years. He's debts were increasing and he wanted to force a reorganization, but he was in even more difficult straits. Therefore, in November of last year, he borrowed 1 million yuan from the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications to repay old debts. This new debt of 1 million yuan had to be repaid at 100,000 yuan per month starting in December of last year, and would be paid off by September of this year. During He's tenure, in addition to repaying the new debt each month, he also repaid a small amount of the old debt. In total, 1.86 million yuan of old debt has been repaid in the past year. Currently, the old debt is only about 2 million yuan. This summer, the provincial government decided to combine offices in order to plan the sale of government property to build a public office building. It is planned to sell four items: the provincial government property in the provincial capital, the lakeside farmland, the wasteland in various counties, and the Hankou property (formerly owned by the Hunan Bank). If all of these properties could be sold, more than 2 million yuan could be obtained, which could be used to build the provincial government building and repay some of the old debt. However, no one has purchased the lakeside farmland, the wasteland in various counties is still under investigation, and the Hankou property also needs to be cleared up. Currently, only the provincial government property in the provincial capital can be sold immediately. This government property includes the provincial granary and the old military governor's office, which could fetch a price of 60,000 or 70,000 yuan, which could be used to build the provincial government building. However, more than 200,000 yuan from the sale of the provincial granary was used by the Civil Affairs Department to build a general hall in Yisuhe and Yiyang for the sake of implementing warehousing, and only a part of the military governor's office was sold due to the high land price, fetching a price of more than 20,000 yuan. In addition, more than 50,000 yuan was taken away by the National Martial Arts Club. The Finance Department's plan to sell government property to repay old debts has become a pie in the sky, so it has no choice but to borrow new debts, extend the loan period, and reduce the interest rate. A month ago, He went to Shanghai and met with the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications. The three banks had previously made a million-dollar loan and had a good credit rating. As a result of the negotiations, a new loan of 1.4 million yuan was agreed upon with the three banks. All the contract signing procedures have been submitted to the provincial government for filing yesterday. The Central Bank of China provided 560,000 yuan, the Bank of China provided 560,000 yuan, and the Bank of Communications provided 280,000 yuan, for a total of 1.4 million yuan.

Wu Dingchang Inspects Cooperative Enterprises in Anhui Province; Plans to Establish Vegetable Oil Branch Factory in Anhui 82

Wuhu Dispatch: Promoting cooperative enterprises is now considered a crucial strategy for rural relief. In the past, Anhui Province had two main cooperative organizations: one was the Rural Cooperative Committee, established according to the directives of the Military Council; the other was the Anhui Rural Cooperative Office, set up by the China International Famine Relief Commission using funds allocated for agricultural relief after the 1931 floods. Currently, the total number of cooperative societies has reached around 3,000, covering over 60 counties across Anhui, with operating funds of about 1.5 to 1.6 million, greatly benefiting the rural areas. Consequently, farmers' confidence in them has deepened. Recently, Minister of Industry Wu Dingchang, recognizing that the China International Famine Relief Commission's Anhui Rural Cooperative Office had been placed under the administration of the Ministry of Industry, and that the Rural Cooperative Committee was already under the Ministry's jurisdiction, sought to consolidate authority and facilitate implementation. He traveled to Anhui for inspection, accompanied by Zhang Yuanshan, Director of the Cooperative Affairs Department, and Zheng Dasheng, Section Chief, aiming to provide guidance and maximize development. Upon arriving in Anqing, they first listened to reports from Wu Jingji, Chief Inspector of the Rural Cooperative Committee, and Yang Xingcun, Director of the Office. Accompanied by Liu Yiyan, Director of the Anhui Construction Department, they inspected cooperative societies in the suburbs of Anqing, including Gao Hebu and Huang Gu Zui. Subsequently, accompanied by Director Liu and others, they departed along the Nanjing-Hefei Road, conducting detailed inspections in Shucheng, Tongcheng, and Hefei counties and towns in central Anhui. From Hefei, they traveled via the Huainan Railway, passing through Chaoxian and Hanshan, arriving in Wuhu yesterday. Yang Mianzhong, Director of the Anhui Finance Department, also awaited them in Wuhu. Directors Liu and Yang, along with local leaders, held a welcoming banquet at the Sun Yat-sen Memorial Hall on Zheshan Mountain. During the banquet, Minister Wu highly praised the effective cooperative enterprises in Anhui Province and expressed satisfaction with the economic construction. He pledged to provide substantial assistance to complete all plans for economic construction and rural cooperation throughout Anhui. Wu departed by car for Nanjing that evening, while Director Liu of the Construction Department boarded a river steamer that afternoon to return directly to Anqing. Before leaving, he told reporters that the vegetable oil factory established by the Ministry of Industry would initially focus on refining tung oil to develop foreign trade. However, Anhui Province's tung oil production is only 30,000 to 50,000 dan per year, which is quite limited. The local need is for refining rapeseed oil, with recent annual exports exceeding 300,000 dan, sold primarily to Japan. Therefore, a positive study on refining rapeseed oil is necessary. Experts are currently inspecting Anhui, and a decision on whether to establish a vegetable oil branch factory in Anhui will be made in the very near future. (8th)

Amidst Agricultural Bumper Harvests, Hubei Province Treasury Revenue Gradually Increases; Total Tax Revenue for the First Half of the Year Reaches 3.2 Million Yuan; Land Deeds Increase, Business and Brokerage Taxes Decrease 83

Hankou Dispatch: With bumper harvests in Hubei Province this year, rural finance is showing some activity, and there is hope for a gradual increase in provincial treasury revenue. According to a recent survey of various tax revenues for the past six months: (1) Actual land tax revenue was over 1,050,000 yuan; (2) Actual deed tax revenue was over 458,000 yuan; (3) Actual business tax revenue was over 1,179,000 yuan; (4) Actual brokerage tax revenue was over 47,000 yuan; (5) Actual slaughter tax revenue was over 168,000 yuan; (6) Actual tobacco and alcohol license tax revenue was over 51,000 yuan; (7) Actual public property revenue was over 237,000 yuan. The total revenue was 3.2 million yuan. The land tax revenue increased by over 100,000 yuan compared to the amount collected last year. This is despite the fact that many counties requested exemptions due to floods and droughts last year, and many county governments did not report the allocation of collection fees to the treasury for accounting. Otherwise, the increase would have been even greater. The provincial government is now exerting its full effort to rectify the situation, and future revenue should improve further. Deed tax revenue increased by over 76,000 yuan compared to the second half of last year because the government showed consideration for disaster victims and waived penalties for late tax payments on unregistered deeds, encouraging many people to register. However, business tax, brokerage tax, slaughter tax, tobacco and alcohol license tax, and public property revenue all fell short of expectations due to consecutive years of disasters, rural bankruptcy, weak consumption, and commercial decline. Business tax was short by over 105,000 yuan, brokerage tax was short by over 26,000 yuan, slaughter tax was short by over 90,000 yuan, tobacco and alcohol license tax was short by over 12,000 yuan, and public property revenue was short by over 13,000 yuan. While this is unavoidable during the rectification process, the main reason remains the disasters. Therefore, the government still relies on central subsidies to cover expenses. Fortunately, this year is a bountiful year, and future tax revenues will definitely increase daily. (September 7th)

Suzhou: Principal Offender in Robbery Case Arrested 84

In the Houtang Shuiqiao area of Xiangshan in Suzhou, the homes of village chief Zhou Jiarong and three others were robbed late at night on the 6th, resulting in significant losses. In addition to burning the victim, the pursuing police officer Li Shanxin was shot and injured. On the 7th, the Public Security Bureau, under the strong supervision of Inspector Wei, led a team to the countryside to pursue and suppress the bandits. On the 8th, Chen Mingchang, the principal offender in the case, was arrested. The suspect had previously served as a member of the Xukou Security Corps. Victim Zhou Jiarong identified him at the scene as the perpetrator who burned his wife's lower body. He was immediately taken into custody, along with four other suspects, including Zhong Shuisheng, and sent to the Public Security Bureau to await interrogation.

Suspect Arrested in Murder Case 85

As reported in this newspaper, an elderly widow, Zhang Li, living alone in Hansha Village, Hengjing, was murdered for her savings, which were coveted by bandits. It is now learned that on the 8th, the District Procuratorate sent Prosecutor Zhou to the countryside to conduct an autopsy. The autopsy confirmed that she had been killed. Based on the terrain, it appeared that the bandits had entered the house by climbing over the roof and escaped towards Taihu Lake. However, the deceased had a foster son, Jin Yusheng, who was known to associate with undesirable individuals and was considered a prime suspect. He has been arrested and taken to the bureau. At the same time, a habitual thief, Lu Ashui, was also arrested on suspicion. Both were sent to the District Court for interrogation on the 9th.

To nominate representatives to petition in Nanjing, striving to reduce the collection of improvement fees and business taxes. The cocoon permits previously issued to cocoon merchants in various counties of Jiangsu province are about to expire. It should be requested from the provincial authorities to continue their reissuance to maintain business; 6. The price of autumn cocoons in this session will be based on the price agreed upon by Zhejiang and Wuxi; 7. Autumn cocoon association fees will continue to be handled in the same manner as spring cocoons; 8. The association's finances are strained. Fees should be collected according to the resolved fee standards after the autumn cocoons are weighed, along with any outstanding amounts from the spring season, to continue the association's operations.

United Effort to Oppose Housing Levy 87

Regarding the case of Jiangsu Province collecting a housing levy from residents, the Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce has previously telegraphed the Provincial Government and Ministry of Finance, urging a swift halt based on the "Provisional Measures for Reorganizing Housing Levies in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province." Yang Bangyan and Li Shuren, along with Chen Shiruo and Wu Shanpei, gentry of Zhenjiang, noted that the Zhenjiang County Government had included the housing levy in its budget and would soon begin collecting it. They also sent telegrams to the Ministry and Province based on the law, striving to achieve the goal of abolishment. Furthermore, the Gaoyou Chamber of Commerce received a reply from the Ministry of Finance stating that the Provincial Government had been consulted to handle the matter in accordance with Article 10 of the approved measures. Therefore, although the county had issued new regulations for the housing levy, the housing levy had not been implemented. They have now sent a letter to the Wuxi Chamber of Commerce to inform them of this.

Jiangyin: Young Woman Suddenly Hangs Herself 89

Ding Wenhan, a farmer from Zhujiaxiang, Changshou Kunshan Township, 2nd District, Jiangyin, married to Shi, is a couple in their fifties. They only have one daughter, named Lindi, who is 21 years old and not yet betrothed. Her mother suffers from a nervous illness. Her father, longing for a son, married a widow surnamed Hu as a concubine this spring. Her relationship with the daughter was good. Yesterday (the 8th), at around 2:00 PM, Lindi suddenly went to her own room and hanged herself with a rope. It is said that the reason for her suicide was a marriage problem.

Nantong: Corpse Causes Uproar at Market in Murder Case 90

The prosecutor's office dispatched a bailiff to the city to examine the body. The local people, wanting to seek justice for the deceased, refused to let them take the body. The market was in uproar. As a result, only Shan Zhigang and his daughter were taken to the court to await further instructions.

Completion of Lianyungang Longhai Electric Plant 92

Since construction of the Lianyungang Longhai Electric Plant began last year, the building was completed by April this year. However, the installation of internal machinery was not immediately completed, so they rushed to install it overnight. By the end of August, the installation was finally complete. The plant manager telegraphed several British engineers from the Shanghai Electric Plant to come to the port to inspect the machinery and supervise the trial run. It is said that the machine is the latest invention of British electric machinery, worth over 200,000 yuan. The trial run was conducted on the evening of the 4th, and there were no problems. The magnitude of its horsepower and the brightness of its light need not be elaborated. However, because the Huangwo Dam has not been completed, the water supply, although stored, is still inconvenient. It is truly a fly in the ointment. It is now scheduled to begin sending electricity at the end of September, when the poles along all roads are fully installed.

Collapse of Lianyungang Sea Wall 93

Recently, the weather in Lianyungang has been intermittently cloudy and sunny, with frequent hurricanes. Today (the 5th), the sea also experienced high tide. For a time, strong winds and huge waves crashed directly against the coast, splashing waves tens of feet high, sounding like thousands of horses galloping. In an instant, the wave-blocking wall of Pier No. 1 collapsed completely, stretching over twenty zhang. Seawater rushed to the warehouses on the pier. The coastal walls east of the pier also collapsed in many places. The loss to the project is quite substantial.

Jiaxing: Robbers Intercept Farmers' Boat 94

Mo Baochen, a villager from Mojiahui outside the North Gate of Jiaxing, aged 64, and his son Mo Yinshou, rowed their own farm boat on the morning of the 8th, loaded with one dan of rice and cash, to repay rent to Li Ruichen in Wangjiangjing. While passing the Jinqiao area of Wangjiangjing Tang, they were suddenly met by two small boats. There were five people in the boats, who blocked their way, ordered them to stop, and beat Mo Baochen with oars. As a result, they robbed all one dan of rice and 93.7 yuan of cash they carried. They immediately went to the Beiping Township Office and the Tangwan Street Police Station to report the case for investigation.

Suddenly, more than ten pirates came and kidnapped the ship and people. It has been ten days since then, and there has been no news. Family members such as Qiu Bingji reported to the county government yesterday, requesting that a team be sent to rescue them.

Commemoration of Premier's First Uprising; City Party Headquarters Held a Grand Meeting Yesterday; All Sectors of the City Celebrated by Displaying Flags 97

Guomin News Agency reports: Yesterday (the 9th) was the 42nd anniversary of Premier Sun's first uprising in Guangzhou. The city party headquarters specially convened a grand meeting in its auditorium, attended by over 200 people, including representatives from all district party headquarters, district sub-branches, and all staff members of the headquarters. Committee member Huang Zaoxiong chaired the meeting, Zhang Hanyun served as master of ceremonies, and Du Mengsen recorded the proceedings. After performing the rituals, Chairman Huang Zaoxiong delivered a report, stating in essence that today is the 41st anniversary of the Premier's first uprising. Recalling this day 41 years ago, the Premier's emotions were undoubtedly tense, and the sacrifices of the martyrs, who bravely marched forward and disregarded their own safety, were incredibly tragic and passionate. Therefore, we should especially commemorate this anniversary, which marks the beginning of overthrowing the Manchu Qing government and establishing the Republic of China. However, can the revolution of these past 41 years be considered a success? Should our comrades still strive for further progress? In my opinion, the revolution cannot yet be considered a success, and comrades must continue to work hard. Internally, we must eliminate the Communist Party and strive for construction; externally, we must abolish unequal treaties to complete the Premier's unfinished revolutionary work. The only somewhat comforting aspect is that the Guangxi issue has been resolved peacefully. The forces of local separatism that have existed for over 20 years can be destroyed, and the hope of unifying China and presenting a united front to the outside world is not difficult to achieve. Soon, the National Assembly will be convened, the Constitution will be promulgated, and constitutional governance will begin, marking the successful conclusion of the Premier's revolutionary cause. Today, we commemorate the Premier's first uprising; in the future, we will celebrate the success of the revolution. With this, we wish the Republic of China long life. All agencies, organizations, schools, and party headquarters at all levels throughout the city uniformly displayed flags yesterday to celebrate.

Sino-French Airmail Express; Shanghai to Paris in Ten Days

Waibun News Agency translated from the French Shanghai Daily: Air traffic between China and France began at the start of this year, but was unfortunately temporarily suspended due to the conflict between Nanjing and Guangzhou. However, it has now fully resumed its original state, and letters sent from Shanghai can reach Paris in ten days. It is reported that mail sent from Shanghai on August 20th arrived in Paris on August 30th, and letters from Paris on August 27th arrived in Shanghai on September 6th. The route taken by these airmail letters is: the transportation between Shanghai and Guangzhou is handled by China National Aviation Corporation; the transportation between Guangzhou and Hanoi is handled by Southwest Aviation Corporation; and the transportation between Hanoi and Paris is handled by Air France. As for those who send this airmail, if it is express mail, it must be mailed by 11:00 PM on Wednesday evenings; if it is regular mail, it must be mailed before 2:00 AM on Thursday mornings. It is also reported that an airmail mailbox has been set up at the corner of Rue du Consulat and Quai de France in the French Concession.

Following legal procedures, each group publicly inspected the ballot boxes' seals. The seals were then broken, and each ballot was read aloud and recorded. This process concluded around 4:00 PM. The elected candidates, in accordance with Appendix 3 of the Election Law, Article 20 of the same law, and Article 19 of the Implementing Rules of the Election Law, represent three times the number of representatives to be elected. This amounts to 12 members from the farmers' association (including the fishermen's association), 12 members from the labor union (including 3 members selected by the maritime workers' union), and 12 members from the chamber of commerce (including the shipping guild). According to law, once the municipal election supervisor reviews the qualifications, a roster will be submitted to the National Assembly Election Headquarters, which will then forward it to the National Government, specifying three times the number of people. China General Chamber of Industry Federation Sends Telegram to the Executive Yuan and Ministry, Requesting the Abolition of the Ji-Cha Inspection Office and the Severe Punishment of Those Who Proposed or Promoted Its Implementation 99

The China General Chamber of Industry Federation in this city, due to the Ji-Cha Political Affairs Committee levying new taxes on smuggled goods and having formally established an inspection office, telegraphed the Executive Yuan and the Ministries of Finance and Industry again yesterday, requesting strict sanctions and ordering its abolition. The original text reads: "Nanjing Executive Yuan, Ministry of Finance, Ministry of Industry, your esteemed consideration: The Ji-Cha authorities initially denied the establishment of an inspection office, or claimed that, although there was such a proposal, it had actually been abandoned. Now, the inspection office has actually been found to be located at No. 8 Xujia Building, Hua'an Street, Special District 2, Tianjin, and is preparing for its establishment, starting on September 1st. The director and deputy director are Wang Hongen and Yuan Chonghuan, respectively, and they have openly and formally hosted the Tianjin press. This is a fact and cannot be concealed. According to the written statement issued by the inspection office (Shen Bao, September 7th, special dispatch), it is planned to investigate smuggled goods that have been smuggled into the mainland without paying customs duties, and to collect inspection fees to regulate market prices and maintain legitimate merchants. This is only a temporary expedient. Once the government has a solution, it will be stopped, and so on. This is a reversal of right and wrong, confusing black and white, and is extremely absurd. Investigating tax-evading smuggled goods is a violation of national laws and should be strictly investigated and dealt with. The National Government has already promulgated anti-smuggling regulations, and penalties should be imposed accordingly. All smuggled goods found should be confiscated and fines imposed and punished. How can they be investigated and then released after collecting inspection fees? It is inappropriate to release them, and even if the inspection fees are 'discretionary,' the amount collected must be very small. Smugglers have already violated the law, and those who find smuggled goods but do not handle them in accordance with national laws and arbitrarily collect handling fees and release them are also violating the law. Strictly speaking, it is like collusion and should be jointly punished. Moreover, smugglers are like thieves. How can there be a reason to call thieves legitimate merchants? Thieves are arrested and brought to justice, and they deserve what they get. Now, there are those who pity the thieves who have nowhere to place their stolen goods and actually find ways to clear them out and collect inspection fees, allowing them to sell the goods. Then, what is the difference between those who collect fees and those who sit on the ground and share the loot? If they reward the style of thieves and regard tax evasion as a legitimate business, then those who abide by the law and pay taxes will be worse than thieves. How can there be such a reason in the world? The anti-smuggling regulations promulgated by the National Government are the government's solution to tax evasion. How can other solutions be proposed? This is clearly a misrepresentation. The major cause of the decline in market prices is the proliferation of tax-evading goods. Legitimate merchants suffer losses and cannot maintain their business. The entry of tax-evading goods into the mainland comes from North China. North China cannot stop smuggling and strictly reject smuggled goods. Instead, it helps its fierce flames. They still say, 'To regulate market prices and maintain legitimate merchants.' There is no doubt that this is a reversal of black and white. The Chinese-owned yarn factories in Tianjin have been sold to Japanese merchants due to the dumping of tax-evading cotton yarn, resulting in losses and closures. It has not been heard that the North China authorities have sympathized with their plight and come forward to maintain and rescue them to prevent production from falling into the hands of foreigners. Now, they pay special attention to tax-evading smuggled goods and ease their sales channels. What could be more absurd than this? In their written statement, there are also words such as 'If there are more smuggled goods coming in, the responsibility depends on how the customs fights smuggling.' There is no intention to cooperate in fighting smuggling. Customs in North China is very strict in fighting tax evasion, but it has not been heard that the North China authorities have assisted customs in fighting smuggling. Show this to the whole country. Now, they are setting up this inspection office, which destroys the complete system of national tariffs. What else can be said about their madness? We know that the special environment in North China is extremely difficult, but this concerns the sovereignty of the entire China. How can we forget the national and national concepts and blindly follow others and engage in it? If it is taken by foreign forces, we should resist to the death and call out to redress grievances. Now, they do not hesitate to damage their reputation, do not hear rumors, do not ask right or wrong, and do it calmly, and issue such absurd remarks, no less than showing to China and foreign countries that China's complete tariff system has been destroyed by North China itself, and smuggling work has also been fundamentally eliminated by North China itself. How can the people of the country tolerate it? We should telegraph to the illegal agencies for emergency sanctions, order the North China Political Affairs Committee to transfer the inspection office and abolish it within a deadline, and severely punish those who propose or implement it, in order to extend national law and sovereignty. China General Federation of Industry Standing Committee members Guo Shun, Cai Shengbai, Wang Qiyu, Hu Xiyuan, Zhu Gengtao, bowed, Jia."

China Aviation Association General Headquarters to Close Down Completely at the End of the Month; Aircraft Purchase Donations Also to Cease Simultaneously; One Million Yuan to Be Handed Over to the Government First 102

After the establishment of the National Aviation Construction Association General Headquarters in Nanjing, the China Aviation Association was ordered to close down and merge. On the afternoon of the 8th, the Association held a general meeting of directors in the downtown area. Directors Lin Kanghou, Wang Xiaolai, Wu Tiecheng, Huang Bingheng, Yao Xijiu, etc., were present. Because the number of attendees was insufficient, the meeting was changed to a standing committee meeting, chaired by Wang Xiaolai, to discuss the closing down of association affairs. The following resolutions were made: 1. The China Aviation Association Shanghai General Headquarters and the Shanghai Solicitation Team General Office will be completely closed down by the end of September to facilitate handover. 2. Directors Lin Kanghou (concurrently Secretary-General Yao Xijiu) and Solicitation Team Director-General Li Dachao were appointed to be responsible for handling the handover matters. 3. The Flying Club's flight training class will continue to be conducted until the first class of students graduates at the end of this year, after which it will be closed down. It is recommended that the National Aviation Construction Association continue to run it. 4. The Aviation Bi-monthly Magazine will continue to be published until the end of the year, and it is recommended that the Association continue to publish it. 5. The Aircraft Purchase Birthday Celebration Donation Association will also be closed down by the end of September. The Association handled over 4.5 million yuan in pledged donations, of which 1.5 million yuan has been paid. One million yuan will be handed over to the government first within days. The standing committee was discussed until about 6:00 PM before it was adjourned. Secretary-General Yao was dispatched to Nanjing by overnight train on the 9th to report to the general headquarters, request the dispatch of personnel to Shanghai to take over, and discuss the establishment of a Shanghai branch, etc.

Shaanxi, Shanxi, Hebei This Year's Cotton Marketing Methods: Regulations Stipulate that Members Cooperatively Market Cotton and Pay 70%; Cooperatives Pay 100% for Cotton Purchased 103

New cotton from various parts of our country has been launched this year. The China Agricultural Banking Group, etc., has allocated huge sums of money to handle cotton marketing loans in various provinces. The Marketing General Office of the Central Cotton Improvement Institute, etc., have agreed on the cotton cooperative of Shaanxi, Shanxi, Hebei and other three provinces in the cotton marketing methods of the year 25 as follows: Article 1, the cotton cooperative marketing 70% payment method for members: When members hand in cotton to the cooperative, the cooperative will pay 70% of the cotton price in advance according to the local market price, and then immediately classify and pack the cotton and transport it to the nearest marketing branch, entrust the agency for sale or sell it by the agency itself, and the risk shall be borne by the members. If there is a surplus at the end of the year, members can get cooperative dividends. Article 2, there are two methods for individual marketing with 100% payment of cotton: (1) If the marketing office handles it for the manufacturer at the cooperative, the profit and loss shall be borne by the client, and the cooperative shall only charge a considerable handling fee and enjoy special tax benefits. (2) If the cooperative purchases it with 100% payment and the member's cotton is transported to the nearest marketing office for sale, the profit and loss shall be borne by the cooperative, the member shall not bear the market price risk, and there shall be no cooperative dividends. Regarding the above-mentioned Article 1 and Article 2 (2), special attention should be paid to reducing risk methods, which are listed as follows: (1) The marketing branch calculates according to local market conditions, formulates product standards, and notifies each agency of the price limit at any time, and each agency's valuation of cotton shall be based on the standard product valuation, and shall not exceed the marketing office's limit. (2) Each agency should accept the guidance of the inspectors sent by the marketing office regarding cotton harvesting and marketing operations. (3) The cotton collected by each agency should be packed into bales as soon as possible and transported to the nearest marketing branch for sale, and must not be transported far or stockpiled to avoid risk. The total amount of cotton stored in the agency and in transit and stored in the warehouse designated by the marketing office that has not been sold shall be limited to an average of 100 dan per agency. (4) Whenever a member returns a loan for production, the agency must attach a notice to the cotton when it arrives at the branch (detailed methods will be formulated separately). After the cotton is sold, the principal and interest of the loan for production shall be deducted by the branch and returned to the banking group. (5) For cotton purchased with 70% or 100% payment, the branch shall still pay the selling price to the cooperative after the sale to facilitate turnover. If the warehouse can provide a 70% pledge for the cotton before it is sold, the money obtained from the pledge shall be handed over to the agency to facilitate turnover. After the cotton is sold, the principal and interest of the pledge shall be deducted and the remaining money shall be returned to the cooperative. After receiving the money, the agency shall distribute the remaining money to the members or include it in its own income according to the regulations of the cooperative. (6) During the business marketing period, each agency shall fill in the daily report and send it to the marketing branch every day to facilitate verification of the quantity and price, and to examine the amount of production loans recovered, so that it can be deducted and returned to the banking group.

The Starting Point for Salary Income Tax Is Not Allowed to Be Changed - The Ministry of Finance Responds to the City Federation 104

The Shanghai First Special District Citizens' Federation received a direct instruction from the Ministry of Finance, No. 10667, yesterday: "Reply to the Shanghai First Special District Citizens' Federation's submission on August 14, 25, regarding the earnest request to forward to the Central Government, taking into account the people's sentiments and sympathizing with the lives of lower-level staff, to change the salary income tax to start at 50 yuan or more, in order to alleviate the people's difficulties. The submission is noted. The starting point for the second category of salary and remuneration income is 30 yuan. Considering the ordinary living expenses of people in various parts of our country, and comparing them with the living standards of various countries in the East and West, the standard is still low. Taking 30 yuan as the starting point is not overly strict. Moreover, a tax rate of 5% per 10 yuan is levied on 30 yuan of income. The people will not be burdened by such a slight tax obligation, nor will it affect the livelihoods of individuals or families. The Provisional Regulations on Income Tax and its Implementation Rules have been approved by the Executive Yuan and are scheduled to be implemented from October 1 of this year. The second category of civil servant salary and remuneration income, and the third category of bond deposit interest income will also be levied from October 1, and other items will be levied from January 1, 26. The request to forward the amendments should not be discussed. Please be informed."

The Yangtze River Basin Has a Bumper Harvest; Shipping Suddenly Flourishes, Restoring the Golden Age 105

In recent years, the Yangtze River route, the business of various companies has sharply declined. After the six companies' alliance and public sharing, although the water foot has been raised, there is very little freight. In July of this year, the six companies planned to reduce the number of shifts, average freight, and organize a Yangtze River inspection team to try to reverse the decline. However, due to Nichi Qing's opposition, this matter was not realized. However, because of the bumper harvest along the Yangtze River, the shipping industry suddenly turned around. All the farmland in the provinces of the Yangtze River Basin and the counties around Dongting Lake had a lower water level, and with favorable weather conditions, all crops were harvested at 100%. The early rice transported to Shanghai has arrived like a tide, part of which is transshipped to Shantou and Guangdong, and part of which is stored in Shanghai. In Changsha, new rice is piled up like a mountain, and farmers are eager to sell. Therefore, in the recent weeks, the downstream Yangtze River vessels of the six companies have almost all been loaded with new rice, beans, wheat, etc., and each vessel has been loaded at 100%, and some have even exceeded the load-bearing capacity. For example, the Jianshe steamship ran aground because it was carrying too much cargo. Taking the China Merchants Bureau as an example, the Yangtze River grains piled up in the docks of Jinliyuan Wharf have filled up all the docks. Jiujiang and Wuhu are also shipping new rice to Shanghai from Jiangxi and Anhui, so that the Hakka people in various ports are competing to load agricultural products, which has never been seen before, because if they are one shift behind, the market price will be lower. Unfortunately, the six companies are bound by public constraints and cannot add more vessels. Only Nichi Qing Company has been able to take the opportunity to increase the number of vessels, saying that it will resume the ships that have been suspended, and has been competing to load large quantities of grains from Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and Anhui to Shanghai. Therefore, among the downstream businesses, Nichi Qing is the best, followed by China Merchants, Jardine, Sanbei, Taikoo, and Ning Shao. The six companies are concerned about the large amount of grain on the Yangtze River this year, and have agreed to increase the downstream freight rate by 10% on top of the original rate, which has already been implemented, so that large river vessels can earn as much as 20,000 to 30,000 yuan per trip, at least doubling the income compared to the same period last year. Therefore, the Yangtze River route has been restored to the golden age. At the same time, the water foot of the Sichuan River has also risen, because the construction of the Sichuan River is in full swing. Places that were previously inconvenient to travel to can now be reached, and the market has improved. In addition, after the crackdown on smuggled goods, the sales of domestic goods have gradually recovered. Due to the congestion last year, the companies agreed to increase the freight rate for goods shipped from Shanghai to Chongqing or from Yichang to Chongqing by 10%. The cotton yarn water foot has also been notified to the family to increase from 16 yuan to 18 yuan per piece. It is still unprecedented for the Sichuan River to increase prices during the flood season. People in the shipping industry say that the water foot for transporting Sichuan goods will increase greatly during the dry season soon.

The Four Central Banks' Legal Tender Is Universally Valid Throughout the Country, Not Restricted by the Place Names Printed on the Bills; The Bank of Communications' Banknotes from the Three Northeastern Provinces Are Not Included 108

Since the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Finance that legal tender should be universally valid and not restricted by place names, the Xin Sheng News Agency reporter learned from the four central banks yesterday that the banknotes issued by the Central Bank do not have place names printed on them, except for Shanghai and Chongqing, and are universally valid throughout the country. However, banknotes with the place names of Shanghai and Chongqing are also universally valid throughout the country and are not restricted by the place names. Banknotes of the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications that are commonly used in the market have place names printed on them, but are not restricted by the place names. However, banknotes issued in "Manchukuo" (i.e., the Three Northeastern Provinces), such as Harbin and Fengtian, are not included. The newly issued banknotes of the China Farmers Bank do not have place names printed on them and are universally valid throughout the country. Banknotes with place names issued in the past are also universally valid throughout the country.

Guangdong Province Illegally Confiscates Power Company: Chamber of Commerce Telegraphs for Correction 110

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce yesterday telegraphed Chiang Kai-shek, Director of the Guangzhou Headquarters, and the Ministry of Industry in Nanjing, requesting the correction of Guangdong Province's confiscation of a commercially-run power company in 1932. The original telegram stated: "To Director Chiang of the Guangzhou Headquarters, for transfer to the Ministry of Industry in Nanjing: On the 8th of this month, we received a joint letter from Liang Guben, Li Jitang, Liang Hongxun, Zhou Xiwen, Liang Yuangong, Pan Zhihang, Ma Bonian, and other shareholders of the Guangzhou Power Company, stating: 'Our company was illegally confiscated by the Guangzhou Municipal Government on July 8, 1932, and our capital and advances exceeding ten million yuan have been lost without any resolution. The patent term has also not expired. The shareholders' meeting unanimously resolved to fight to the death, and domestic and overseas organizations advocating public welfare have also appealed on our behalf. The Central Construction Committee issued a dispatch to the Guangdong Provincial Government in November of the same year, ordering a thorough investigation and to cease the confiscation; however, at that time, the warlords were in power and refused to obey the order, so we had to endure in silence until now. We have found that at the Fourth Plenary Session of the 19th year of the Republic (1930), members proposed protecting private enterprises and prohibiting the confiscation of private power companies, which was passed at the Third General Assembly. This glorious resolution should not be a mere formality. Furthermore, in the past, electric light companies in Hankou, Kaifeng, Zhejiang, and other places were also confiscated by local governments, but Director Chiang ordered their return. This demonstrates the government's determination to maintain private enterprises, which has long been known throughout the world. The case of our company is the same, so how can it be treated differently? Now that Guangdong's administration is unified, all local officials must abide by the central government's clear orders. We have submitted a request for the return of our company based on reason and facts. We are extremely grateful for your association's sympathy and assistance in the past. Now that the old matter is being brought up again, we still request that your association continue to telegraph appeals to the authorities to promptly return our company, so as to maintain the central government's authority and protect the people's property. This will be beneficial to China's industry.' Upon arrival, it was found that this matter was discussed by the association on September 3, 1932. The association sent a detailed telegram to the Ministry of Industry (your ministry), clearly stating the company's illegal confiscation by the Guangzhou Municipal Government and the Guangdong Provincial Government's protection of the confiscation. On September 13 of the same year, the association received a reply from the Ministry of Industry (your ministry) with document number 4997, stating that the Guangdong Provincial Government had been requested to provide a detailed reply for verification and handling. However, this matter was ultimately delayed for four years because it was said that there was no legal or factual basis for the claim. The Ministry of Industry (your ministry) was unable to verify and handle the case, resulting in irreparable losses for the shareholders. Now that Guangdong's political orders are unified and follow the central government's directives, all cases of illegal actions in the past that have not been corrected should be investigated and dealt with one by one, so that businessmen can have hope for revival. We hereby submit this situation to your director (ministry) for review and approval, and humbly request that you order the Guangdong Provincial Government to review the original case of the Ministry of Industry in September 1932 and conduct a re-examination and handling of the commercial stock company that should not have been confiscated, in accordance with the law, so as to demonstrate justice and maintain the rule of law. This would be in the public interest. The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce respectfully submits."

Promoting the Notary System: Simplified Procedures 111

According to a report from the National News Agency in this city on the 9th, the current notary system requires that if a notary public officer does not know the applicant, the applicant must present a certificate from the district chief, chamber of commerce, or police chief of the jurisdiction, or have two witnesses known to the officer to prove their identity. This is clearly stipulated in Article 17, Paragraph 1 of the Provisional Rules for Notarization. However, in practice, it takes time and is inconvenient for applicants to directly request certificates from the aforementioned authorities. It is also not easy to find two witnesses known to the officer to prove their identity. Therefore, the promotion of the notary system has many obstacles. Recently, the Minhou District Court submitted a request to the ministry to have the court send a letter to the district chief, chamber of commerce, or police chief to verify that the applicant is indeed the person in question, and the reply letter would be regarded as a certificate; or to have the court send two staff members to investigate and report that the person is indeed the person in question, which would also be regarded as having the effect of a certificate, so as to avoid inconvenience to the applicant and ensure the smooth implementation of the notary system. The Judicial Yuan believes that the proposed method is feasible and has already instructed all courts handling notarization to be informed accordingly.

Anchor Chain Entangles Propeller: Fuhua and Yunchang Vessels Suffer Minor Damage in Wanxian 113

The Sanbei Company's river steamer Fuhua, ordered to proceed to Taipingxi to rescue the Fuyang vessel, arrived at Wanxian at 5:30 PM on the 7th of this month. As usual, it dropped anchor, but because the river water had receded greatly and the sand at the bottom of the river was very thick, it could not move forward. It then began to move backward, but unexpectedly, the right engine propeller became entangled with the anchor chain of the Yunchang vessel. Both ships were affected. The Yunchang vessel, fearing an accident, quickly released its anchor. The Fuhua was then safe, but the Yunchang's anchor chain was entangled in the Fuhua's propeller, and the Fuhua was unable to move. It had to remain anchored at Wanxian and hire divers to go into the water to release the entangled anchor chain before it could sail again. Efforts are being made to salvage the anchor dropped by the Yunchang vessel.

China Plans to Establish Bank in Siam 118

However, Due to Absence of Commercial Treaty, Currently Difficult to Realize

According to Xin Xin She, since the return of the Chinese delegation to Siam, the urgent need to improve Sino-Siamese relations has attracted the attention of the whole country. In order to maintain the inherent economic position of overseas Chinese in Siam, the establishment of a large-scale bank is indeed an urgent matter. Recently, there has been talk that the Bank of China will prepare to establish a branch in Bangkok. The Xin Xin She reporter specially inquired about the truth from the banking community. It is reported that since the return of the political delegation to Siam, it has been generally agreed that cultivating the economic vitality of overseas Chinese and establishing a large-scale bank in Bangkok is an urgent task to rescue the overseas Chinese. There are more than 3 million overseas Chinese in Siam, most of whom are engaged in agriculture and commerce. The economic center of Siam is mostly in the hands of overseas Chinese. In recent years, due to the panic of the world economy and the oppression of various countries, the economic strength has gradually weakened. Although there are Huaqiao Bank and Hua Shang Bank in Siam, they are limited in scale and can hardly serve as the backing for the entire overseas Chinese economy. If it is allowed to develop naturally without self-help, the economy of the overseas Chinese in Siam will eventually be oppressed and collapse. Therefore, the overseas Chinese hope that the country can quickly establish a bank in Siam. However, although the relationship between China and Siam is deep, due to the absence of a commercial treaty, all progress is difficult to begin. Therefore, the most needed thing at present is for the Sino-Siamese commercial treaty to be signed as soon as possible to establish formal diplomatic relations, so that the establishment of a large-scale bank and the relief of overseas Chinese can proceed smoothly.

China Alcohol Factory Drops Prices: Machinery Association Requests Curb 119

According to Shen Shi She, the Machinery Association submitted a report to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Industry, stating that the state-run alcohol factory is dropping prices and competing with private alcohol factories. They earnestly request the Executive Yuan to order the Ministry of Industry to first curb the price drop and then convene both parties to limit production and regulate selling prices based on registered production volume in order to provide relief and avoid competing with the people for profit. According to a letter from member Meilong Spice Factory, "Last year, the China Alcohol Factory drastically reduced prices and squeezed out the same industry. The association kindly forwarded the report to the Ministry of Industry, which ordered the China Alcohol Factory to cooperate with the association and other factories in the spirit of mutual assistance. However, because the China Alcohol Factory proposed harsh and controversial conditions, it did not come to fruition. However, the spirit of impartiality in the association's handling of the matter has made our factory extremely grateful. Now, the China Alcohol Factory is determined to destroy the same industry without end. On August 6 of this year, it continued to drop the price from 8 jiao 5 fen per gallon to 7 jiao 6 fen, and there are rumors that the price will continue to drop. As a factory that claims to promote industry, it has always gone against its claims, which is both infuriating and regrettable. Therefore, our factory's board of directors decided to submit a report to the Ministry of Industry again to curb this practice. Your association is the leading organization for national goods and has always had a love for industry. We respectfully send this letter and hope that your association will continue to pursue this matter and urge the Ministry of Industry to deal with this case quickly so that justice can be done and people's livelihoods can be relied upon. This is not only the good fortune of our factory. We have attached a copy of the document submitted to the ministry. We hope that you will review and approve it." Upon investigation, the competition between the China Alcohol Factory and the same industry is fierce, and the price drop is huge. In May of last year, Meilong, Zhonghua, Xiaguang, and other alcohol factories jointly submitted a letter to the association requesting the government's relief. Subsequently, in July of the same year, the Ministry of Industry issued document number 12752, instructing the association to convene China, Meilong, Xiaguang, Zhonghua, and other four alcohol factories for amicable cooperation many times, which lasted for four months, but it was difficult to reach an agreement. On October 23 of the same year, the situation was reported to the Ministry of Industry for the record. At that time, the selling price of alcohol had dropped from 1 yuan 5 jiao 6 fen to 8 jiao 5 fen, causing Xiaguang and Zhonghua alcohol factories to be unable to maintain operations and close down one after another. Currently, only China and Meilong factories remain. The China Alcohol Factory clearly knows that the selling price of foreign alcohol is above 2 yuan. If domestic alcohol is sold for 1 yuan 5 jiao, it is enough to compete with foreign goods. If there is no ambition to merge private alcohol factories, why drop the price to 8 jiao 5 fen, and now even below 8 jiao? Such endless competition goes against the Executive Yuan's intention to protect industry and encourage production. Our association has always aspired to develop national goods. In this time of national crisis, instead of thinking about competing with foreign countries, it is only thinking about competing internally, which is painful and difficult to bear in silence. However, the China Alcohol Factory is a factory jointly operated by the Ministry of Industry. If we do not earnestly request the Executive Yuan to order the Ministry of Industry to first curb the price drop, convene both parties to limit production and regulate selling prices based on registered production volume, and provide relief, others will not be able to lead and comply. In fact, the government has repeatedly stated that it will never compete with the people for profit. Therefore, we specially submit this report, attaching a copy of Meilong Factory's document submitted to the ministry, and earnestly request that the Executive Yuan review and approve it, and order the Ministry of Industry to convene both parties to formulate measures so that it can be brought into order. The country is fortunate, and the industry is fortunate.

At 9:40 AM on the 2nd of this month, the Shanghai Municipal Council (SMC) Police Department, along with Chinese and Western detectives from the Yangtzepoo Police Station, went to Chaoyang Road to forcibly demolish squatter shacks at No. 488. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Xiao Xiefen visited the Third Criminal Court for review. Chinese detective No. 345 and Indian detective No. 301 testified that he and defendant Gu Luotian both threw stones. Western Detective Chief Blake accused defendant Mrs. Zhang Shi of carrying a chamber pot to wash and throw excrement. Defendant Hu Guangyu, according to Indian detective No. 371, was at the scene but was not seen throwing stones, although another Indian detective saw him throw stones (but did not appear). Zhou Azhang, Zhou Jinbang, Yang Shiyi, Wang Xiaosanzi, Gu Luotian, Lou Wang, and Zhang Shi were each sentenced to six months, with a three-year suspended sentence. Hu Guangyu was fined twenty yuan, with a two-year suspended sentence. Gu Siming is scheduled to be sentenced at 9:00 AM on the 15th. Wang Lukuan and Sun Hankui were granted bail of 500 yuan each during the appeal period.

On the night of the 11th of last month, at approximately 8:00 PM, a black lacquer wicker suitcase was discovered on the sidewalk in front of the English church at No. 74 Suzhou Road. University Student Induces Immature Dancing Girl into Sexual Intercourse - Sentenced to Eight Months Imprisonment, Granted Two-Year Suspended Sentence 124

Chen Xinyuan (also known as Yingquan), a graduate of Fudan University from Guangdong, was accused by the Old Zhabei Police Station in the First Special District Court of having sexual intercourse with a fifteen-year-old girl, Pan Anan (also known as Zhang Peifang, a dancer at the Great Metropolis Dance Hall), in violation of Article 227 of the Criminal Code. Although the complainant, Pan Qinfu, the father of the victim, withdrew the complaint, the case could not be withdrawn and continued to be heard. However, Chen Xinyuan claimed that Pan was already seventeen years old. The age of Pan was critical to determining his guilt in this case. The court ordered an adjournment for further investigation. This was previously reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Feng Shide continued the trial in the First Criminal Court. Chen Xinyuan, accompanied by his defense lawyer Yang Ruinian, appeared in court. Zhou Mengxiong, the principal of the "Meet for Joy" Dance School at No. 18 Huile Lane, was also summoned as a witness. Zhou testified that Pan, accompanied by her father, came to the school to learn to dance around August or September of last year for about a month. She registered under the name Pan Zhenzhen. Because the school did not focus on age, she was not required to fill out a form. However, in casual conversation, she said she was fourteen years old. Police lawyer Wang Yaotang stated that dance halls must report the names, ages, and addresses of all dancers to the local police station on a monthly basis. Therefore, they investigated with the Jing'an Temple Police Station and found that the Great Metropolis Dance Hall reported Zhang Peifang's age as eighteen in July, with her home address as No. 18 Yongji Lane, Masnan Road, but in August, she was reported as sixteen years old. Based on past investigations, Pan's age could not be determined with certainty. Therefore, her claim to be fifteen years old was difficult to prove. Moreover, the defendant and Pan had known each other for more than a year, and their relationship only began recently. It was possible that the defendant waited for her to come of age. Therefore, it could not be said that there was no basis for the defendant's claim that she was seventeen years old. Subsequently, lawyer Yang Ruinian discussed the issue of Pan's age in detail and stated that there was no doubt that Pan was seventeen years old. He requested that the court declare him innocent. After Judge Feng reviewed the facts, he declared the verdict in court: Chen Xinyuan was sentenced to eight months of imprisonment with a two-year suspended sentence for continuous sexual intercourse with a girl under the age of sixteen. Chen expressed his acceptance of the verdict, and police lawyer Wang also stated that he would not appeal. The case was concluded.

Chinese detectives Liu Junjie and Xia Shutang from the Dixwell Road Police Station apprehended a rickshaw puller from Tongzhou named Chen Huqiu at 9:10 AM on the 1st of this month, who was transporting materials for making red pills. Interrogation revealed that a customer with the surname Zhou from the Daqing Chong Company at No. 23 Yunnan Road had hired him to take the goods to a certain place in Caojiadu, but the customer fled at the opportunity. Romance Bankruptcy Case: Settlement Reached, Conciliation Plan Adjudicated, Order for Debtor to Fulfill 127

The sensational Xu Qizhong romance bankruptcy case has been settled by the court, recognizing the validity of the

Conciliation Plan

passed at the third creditors' meeting convened on July 20th. The main text of the First Special District Court's ruling is extracted below. Civil Ruling No. 9, Sheng Yi, 25th Year of the Jiangsu Shanghai First Special District Court. Bankrupt: Xu Qizhong (resident at No. 12, Lane 49, Zhejiang Road). Regarding the bankrupt's proposal of a conciliation plan for bankruptcy case No. 21, Po, 24th Year of the Republic of China, the creditors' meeting has resolved the terms of the conciliation. The court rules as follows: Main Text: Reasons for approving the conciliation in this case: After the bankrupt was declared bankrupt, a third creditors' meeting was held at 10:00 AM on July 20th of this year, on the third floor of the Chinese Industrial Bank, No. 300 Nanjing Road, this city. Eighty creditors attended, representing a total claim amount of 20,033.97 yuan. The bankrupt proposed a conciliation plan with the following

Terms:

(1) Creditors with claims of 300 yuan or less will be repaid 40% in cash by the bankrupt's family. (2) The Wing On Real Estate Company, as a single creditor, will be compensated with the 1,000 yuan in Jiang Zhe Bank stock held as collateral. (3) Creditors with claims above 300 yuan, excluding the Wing On Real Estate Company, will be repaid proportionally from the proceeds of the auction of the bankrupt's assets and the 15,000 yuan in American Austrian Land Company stock promised by the bankrupt's family. (4) If the above plan is fully approved by the third creditors' meeting, the bankrupt's family will appoint a representative to guarantee the fulfillment of the conciliation. After discussion by the attending creditors, the conciliation plan was

Approved by Majority

The results of the vote were: 9 creditors agreed, representing a total claim amount of 22,101.65 yuan; 1 creditor disagreed, representing a claim amount of 3,000 yuan. (Note: This creditor did not declare their claim but participated in the vote.) Since the number of creditors who agreed exceeded half of the attending creditors, and the claim amount they represented also reached more than three-quarters, it was considered approved. The chairman of the creditors' meeting, Judge Zhao Guangju, reported the above situation to the court. Upon reviewing the conciliation terms approved by the creditors' meeting, they were deemed fair. According to Article 135 of the Bankruptcy Law, it should be approved. The ruling is as stated in the main text.

Former Director of the Gansu Opium Prohibition Bureau, Xu Xueseng, Injured by Acid Attack; Many People Involved in the Case; Plaintiff Detained in Another Case 135

Xu Xueseng, a native of Songjiang and former director of the Gansu Opium Prohibition Bureau, was attacked with nitric and hydrochloric acid on Wangzhi Road in the French Concession on the afternoon of March 6th of this year, causing injuries to his face. Merchants of Hujiaqiao Jointly Request Relocation of Vegetable Market for Mutual Benefit of Merchants and Vendors 137

Over seventy businesses on Hujiaqiao Road in the city, including Tongshenmao, Tiansheng, Zengda, Yongshengtai, Nanyang, Taichang, Guangchang, etc., jointly submitted a petition yesterday to the Public Security, Health, Finance, Social Affairs, Public Works, and Public Utilities Bureaus, requesting the relocation of vegetable stalls to maintain the commercial district. The petition to Public Security Director Zhou Wenzhao is recorded as follows: "Petition regarding the decline of the market, the difficulty of maintaining business, and the request to move the Tianbao Branch Road vegetable market to this road for the mutual benefit of merchants and vendors. The undersigned businesses are all located along Hujiaqiao Road, engaged in commerce. However, business is uneven. Since January 28th, the market has been declining year by year. Furthermore, the economic panic has caused many businesses on this road to be unable to sustain themselves. Many storefronts are vacant. If there is no rescue method, we will inevitably be doomed. We understand that the Tianbao Branch Road vegetable market has been instructed by your bureau to relocate to the Tiande Road area. Although this is being implemented, the vendors believe that the Tiande Road area is remote and that their livelihood is difficult. They have requested relocation to this road, and several petitions have been filed but not approved. Therefore, the undersigned businesses, for the sake of maintaining the market, in addition to submitting petitions to the Health, Finance, Social Affairs, Public Works, and Public Utilities Bureaus, and the Linping Road Police Station, dare to request your Excellency's inspection and approval to relocate the Tianbao Road vegetable market to the Hujia Road area, from Xiangyan Bridge to Tiantong Road Bridge, for the benefit of both vendors and businesses. The Hujiaqiao Road area is neither a major thoroughfare nor has any other obstructions. If you approve, we will be immensely grateful." Respectfully presented to Cai, Director of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau.

According to Dagong News Agency, the Hongxing Sock Factory on Caishi Road in the French Concession has over 400 male and female workers. They petitioned party and government agencies for assistance. After mediation, the eight cadres of the branch, including Deng Yixin, voluntarily resigned, and the issue was resolved. However, the factory's female worker Li Asi had a conflict with Wang Xiuying the day before yesterday, and the factory director Ge Shousheng, after hearing one-sided remarks, dismissed Wang Xiuying. All the workers believed that Li Asi had been used by the factory in the past to sabotage the labor union. To resolve the dispute, the factory should have dismissed both female workers at the same time, but the factory refused this request and moved Wang Xiuying's machine. When the female workers entered the factory yesterday morning, they were furious. They demanded an explanation from the factory but received no results, and a dispute arose.

Conflict Occurs

At approximately 8:00 AM yesterday morning, the factory, seeing the large number of workers and the serious situation, immediately closed the factory doors. At the same time, factory staff members Xia Depei, Le Runtin, Shi Jifu, and others grabbed the hair of female workers Wang Xiuying, Zhang Xiuying, and Zhou Linbao in the crowd and dragged them to the accounting room. The other female workers Wang Xiumei, Zhang Xiuying, and Zhou Linbao were also seriously injured, but the factory refused to send them to the hospital and confined them in the factory. Other victims included Wu Wanzhen, Lu Qinxiang, Zhang Fengxian, Lu Jinmei, Chen Zhaodi, Kang Xiuzhen, Wei Xingxian, Sun Aju, Zhou Ermei, Zhang Huizhen, Wang Chunmei, Zhu Xinghua, Ge Wangshu, etc., but their injuries were minor and not serious.

Authorities Investigate Thoroughly

After receiving the report, the Municipal Party Headquarters and the General Labor Union also sent Li Weixiong and Wan Banghe to the factory to investigate thoroughly and persuade both parties to wait for a resolution and not allow the situation to escalate further. The seriously injured female workers Wang Xiuying, Zhang Xiuying, and Zhou Linbao were not sent to the hospital due to the factory's refusal, and they are still lying in the factory's alleyway, unable to sit up.
