Workers at British, American, and Japanese Factories Resumed Work Yesterday Morning; Conditions Negotiated Voluntarily by Both Parties; Labor and Management Discuss Resolution Steps 144

According to the Public News Agency, all the striking workers at the Third Factory of the British American Tobacco Company (i.e., Zhongyuan Tobacco Company) on Daopeng Road in Pudong, Shanghai, resumed work in the factory yesterday morning after being persuaded by members of the Municipal General Labor Union. The conditions requested will be negotiated voluntarily by both parties. All Chinese and Western detectives stationed in the factory have been withdrawn. The labor unrest that has lasted for more than twenty days can be temporarily resolved. The details are recorded as follows:

Resumed Work Yesterday Morning

Representatives of each department representing all the workers in the factory, after being earnestly persuaded by members of the Municipal General Labor Union, immediately notified the workers to resume work overnight. All the workers successively entered the factory to resume work at 9:30 AM yesterday morning. At the same time, the factory also sounded the whistle to start work. The order was very good when the workers entered the factory to resume work. The factory also expressed its gratification at the workers' resumption of work.

Direct Negotiations

Regarding the eight demands put forward by the labor side, the labor and management sides agreed to hold consultations at 3:00 PM yesterday afternoon, with several responsible representatives elected by the labor side and the English supervisor of the big gang, Hubrook. As a result, the labor side retreated on the personnel part (i.e., Wei Ziqian), but the factory admitted to reinstating the dismissed female workers. Regarding the request for leave procedures and wages during the dispute period, the factory agreed to allow Zhejiang Province to formulate silk control and management committees to supplement the silkworm industry funds, which would be submitted to the Ministry of Industry and the Executive Yuan for approval. The improved seed fresh cocoons produced in this province would be charged an improvement fee of 1.8 yuan per ancestral seed. Now, in order to standardize the price of silkworm seeds and increase the advance payment, the improved seed fresh cocoon seed funds and improvement fees have been submitted to the Zhejiang Provincial Government for approval, and the levy has been increased to 2 yuan per ancestral seed, which was implemented starting in the summer. The autumn fresh cocoons will be on the market soon, and the summer method of levying an improvement fee of 2 yuan per dan of improved seed fresh cocoons will still be followed. According to Xin Xin News Agency reporters, the Shanghai, Wuxi, and Zhejiang silk factory associations believe that the cocoon industry has not recovered, and the improvement fees are still increasing, which silk cocoon manufacturers will not be able to afford. The joint meeting of cocoon vocational associations in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces decided to request the Zhejiang Provincial Government to exempt them, and it is learned that the manufacturers specially appointed Chen Dongshi, Xu Xingbin, and Zhou Yangsong to contact the Zhejiang Provincial Silkworm Silk Control Association to register the number of cocoons received, which should be based on the total registered dan number of the cocoon merchants, not on the individual cocoon lines, so that when the cocoon is abundantly harvested, it can be calculated in a unified manner. cocoon panicle lack, the number of cocoons varies from place to place, and it is difficult to obtain accurate numbers in advance.

Letter 146

I checked today (9th), the news published in the newspapers about the resumption of work of the workers in the Zhongyan Tobacco Factory, and the truth of the facts are quite different. This time, in addition to the fact that the Bureau had approved the order early on, when the union representative Zhou Yuxiang and others went to the municipal government yesterday (8th), Secretary-General Yu cutely told them in person. It is the most important reason for promoting the resumption of work of the factory workers. The previous process has not been described, and should be corrected to avoid misunderstandings. The so-called second convocation of mediation at 9 am today (9th) is even more untrue. The Director of this Bureau is deeply concerned that the expansion of the factory's labor unrest may affect public security, so he ordered the person in charge of the section to telegraph Zhou Xuexiang of the Fourth District Rolled Tobacco Industry Union to come to the Bureau this morning (9th) to urge him to persuade the workers to resume work first and wait for mediation, not to convene mediation. A special letter is hereby requested for correction to clarify the details. Sincerely, Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, September 9,

Directly, I checked the news carried in your newspaper on August 28 about the Chamber of Intestines' petition to the Ministry of Finance to stop the two factories from cheating, accusing this firm's Dinghai branch of carrying private salt when shipping sausage casings. How alarmed I am. All the sausage casings made by our factory are shipped overseas. To prevent them from rotting, they must be salted. According to the regulations of the International Trade Bureau of the Shanghai Industrial Department, each pig intestine needs 5 shi dan to 6 shi dan of salt for 1,500 pairs of pig intestines, 13.5 yards per pair, or 1,250 pairs, 27 yards per pair, or 340 pairs, 100 yards per pair. On August 23, someone falsely reported to the second district of the Suwu tax police bureau, and then took away many barrels of goods shipped by our factory to Shanghai for inspection. As a result of the inspection, barrel No. 83 contained 2,850 pairs of pig intestines, with only 105 jin of pickled salt used, which is far from the amount of salt that should be used. It was sent back by the section, and the suspicion of carrying private salt was pure slander. Furthermore, our industry has not heard of the organization of a peer association. According to the Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Overview compiled by the Shanghai China Credit Institute, there are only four Chinese peers in our industry, in addition to our factory and Chengda, there are now only Gongji, Bairan, Zhonghua, and Shenji. According to Article 3 of the Industrial and Commercial Trade Association Law, the establishment of a trade association must be initiated by seven or more companies and firms in the same industry before it can be established in accordance with the law. As for the so-called Shanghai Intestine Industry Association, our factory belongs to the same industry. Where has the association been established and where is it located? , so far I have not heard of it. However, it has been pointed out that our factory established a factory in Dinghai to marinate sausage casings, which is said to be carrying private salt, which is obviously intended to undermine our factory's business. In addition to investigating in accordance with the law, a corresponding letter is hereby requested. Your newspaper will publish this letter in the letter column in lieu of correction. Sincerely, Wu Lihou, manager of Hanli Huaxing, Shanghai newspaper, September 8,

The Last Four Years (4) of Central University 155

— Luo Jialun

Regarding equipment, from September of the 21st year to June of the 23rd year, the actual expenditure was 246,819 yuan. From July of the 23rd year to June of the 25th year, the actual expenditure was 589,578 yuan. Chemical reagents, etc., listed under consumables, were not included. Therefore, the actual expenditure on equipment in four years reached 836,397 yuan. In total, the actual expenditure on books and equipment in the past four years has reached 1,207,042 yuan. Adding the cost of construction, books and equipment, the total expenditure in the past four years is 1,876,030 yuan.

5. Implement Streamlining and Savings in Administrative Expenses for Construction

The school's funding has been reduced after reorganization and has not increased in the past four years. If construction is desired, it is necessary to reduce personnel and save administrative expenses. After four years of effort, there have been some minor but observable effects. The number of staff in the 24th year was reduced by 76 compared to the 18th year and by 72 compared to the 19th year (the number of staff in the former medical and business colleges has been removed, while the current medical college and dental specialty school staff have been included). Due to further streamlining in the 24th year, the actual reduction compared to the 23rd year was 13 people. As for the number of teachers (including professors, lecturers, and teaching assistants), the number in the 24th year was reduced by 62 compared to the 18th year and by 85 compared to the 19th year. As for administrative expenses, there is no way to verify the figures for the 18th and 19th years, and the numbers are difficult to track down. After the reorganization in the 21st year, there was a major reduction. From the 21st year to the 24th year, the pressure gradually tightened, and there were some results. Administrative expenses accounted for 10.5% of the total budget in the 21st year, reduced to 9.5% in the 22nd year, 9% in the 23rd year, and 8% in the 24th year. These results all came from gradual accumulation over time. From the 21st year to the 23rd year, the school was able to achieve the above-mentioned construction without receiving special funding, which was not without reason.

6. Reorganizing Curriculum

University curriculum in our country is often filled with numerous courses, lacking an organic structure. The school's various departments have separately redefined educational guidelines and reorganized the curriculum, so that required and elective courses have clear regulations and are not changed due to individuals or events. Once the core of the curriculum is formed, the meaning of teaching can be clarified. Thanks to the efforts and assistance of the deans, department heads, and professors, this work was largely completed after a long period of discussion lasting a year. Afterwards, it was revised from time to time based on actual situations. The types of courses have been deleted and merged in many places, and efforts have been made to enrich the content.

In the 24th year, the school added a medical college, a dental specialty school, and a special mechanical research class. The curriculum settings were all based on the standards issued by the Ministry, the curriculum settings of the relevant departments of universities abroad, and the actual needs of the country were carefully formulated, making the whole school's curriculum an organic link.

7. Concentrating Scholars and Emphasizing Full-Time Positions

Scholarship is inherently a specialized undertaking, and those who serve as professors should devote themselves to it wholeheartedly. The school has often felt empty due to years of chaos. At the beginning of the reorganization, it made every effort to retain the original good professors and recruited specialized scholars from time to time. Over the years, many professors and lecturers have been added successively, and the faculty of each department has been largely filled. In the future, we will continue to pay attention at any time and attract talents from all sides, so that the school can become a general gathering of various academic and specialized talents. At the same time, it is even more important to establish a principle of never hiring part-time staff when full-time staff can be hired. The results of the implementation have been quite effective. In the past, the school had as many as 111 part-time teachers. After Jialun arrived at the school, he worked hard to reduce them. In the 21st year, there were 81 part-time teachers, which was reduced to 80 in the 22nd year, 75 in the 23rd year, and only 34 in the 24th year. These few part-time teachers are all experts in certain special sciences and are relied upon by the government or other academic institutions. The school wants to recruit them, but it is impossible in reality. It is deeply grateful to them for sharing a portion of their energy and time to assist the school. From the 15th year onwards, all grades were complete, and the increase or decrease of courses was mostly undertaken by the original teachers, whose enthusiasm is admirable.

8. Emphasizing Moral Education (1) Establishing a Moral Education Committee

In recent years, university education in the country has mostly focused on the infusion of knowledge while neglecting the cultivation of students' character. The school, aware of this, is striving to correct this error. Usually, appropriate guidance is given to students' extracurricular activities and daily life. Over the past four years, thanks to the effective teaching of the professors and the students' self-improvement, the school's atmosphere has changed greatly, and the school's reputation has gradually increased. In order to unify the direction of moral education, a Moral Education Committee was established last September to coordinate all moral education matters. All matters such as formulating various moral education regulations, guiding students' extracurricular activities, evaluating students' conduct grades, reviewing student rewards and punishments, and assisting military management are all handled by the committee, so that students' pursuit of knowledge and cultivation of personality, as well as the habit of group life, can be developed in a balanced way, so as to cultivate a good academic atmosphere and healthy citizens.

(2) Implementing Military Management In order to cultivate students' militarized life, disciplined action, and unified spirit, the school has implemented military management since the 24th year. First-year students who are currently receiving military training are all wearing uniforms and are subject to military management. Military management regulations have been formulated, a military management office has been organized, and a moral education committee and a brigade headquarters have been established to handle all training management and moral education matters. White Goose Painting School Opens 163

The painting training school affiliated to the famous art group White Goose Painting Society will start its study program on September 10th. The school aims to adapt to the amateur study of those who are generally engaged in their duties and love art. It was jointly founded by painters Chen Qiucao, Fang Xuelu, and Pan Siyue. The guidance is detailed and not pretentious. Many of the graduates of previous sessions have been used in practice and have a good reputation. This summer, it moved to the community address at No. 3, Lane 364, Chengdu Road, Avenue Edward VII, because it is located in a thoroughfare and is convenient for scholars. Recently, many people have registered. As for the subjects, in addition to pencil, charcoal, pastel, watercolor, and oil painting, decorative circular design and advertising have also been added to meet social needs. It is still divided into day and night classes. The day class is from 2:00 PM to 5:00 PM, and the night class is from 7:00 PM to 10:00 PM. Whether or not they have studied before, they can join. Due to location, there are not many places available. Those who are interested in art can register as soon as possible. A reply with two points of postage will be sent immediately.

Shanghai Fine Arts College Arts and Crafts Museum Established 164

Since Principal Liu returned to China last year, the Shanghai Fine Arts College has been determined to rectify the school's administration and create a new look. The Ministry of Education sent personnel to inspect the school, and it was considered to be well-managed. This year, a special equipment subsidy of 5,000 yuan was granted to expand the factory's machinery and musical instruments, famous carving models, etc. The school's art education department's drawing and craft group and the pattern department, in addition to the machinery and equipment for the metalworking, woodworking, and silverworking classrooms, which have been ordered by the China Industrial Machinery Factory, have also established an Arts and Crafts Museum next to the Art Museum to display one ancient crafts, two local folk crafts, three craft reference materials, four craft raw materials, and five past student craft achievements. The items are all rare in the world and will be open for exhibition today.

Our Participation in the World Games National Arts Performance Honor 168

Chu Minyi, a member of the Central Committee, came to Shanghai the day before yesterday. A reporter from the Central News Agency interviewed him and talked about the performance of our country's national arts at the World Games. The situation is briefly described as follows: Although we did not get a score, this trip was originally for sightseeing, so we should be able to seek progress through comparison. Among them, the national arts also performed at the conference and in various places, which won a good reputation and was comforting. He also showed a letter from a member from Germany, which described the experience in detail. The following is an excerpt: (Omitted above) The World Games started on August 2nd. Our country's sports all fell behind. On the day the national arts team arrived in Berlin, the entire German Student Association accompanied them to Hamburg to participate in the World Music, Art, and Martial Arts performances. As a result of our performance, we won the welcome of tens of thousands of spectators. On July 27th, we also performed national arts and Tai Chi exercises and Tai Chi balls at the welcome meeting for overseas Chinese students in Berlin, and distributed hundreds of copies of Tai Chi exercise publications. Many German military and political dignitaries attended the meeting that day. The news was published in the newspapers on the same day, with many praises. Later, they went to German military camps to perform various boxing techniques. German soldiers and officials unanimously praised them and distributed Tai Chi exercise publications to them. On August 11th, our national arts team officially performed at the conference. First, there was a group Tai Chi exercise, followed by individual boxing and pair boxing by each member, and finally a weapon performance, all of which were very exciting and won the appreciation of tens of thousands of spectators, with applause and cheers lasting for a long time. On the 17th, Cheng Tian'en sent off all the members. During the meeting, Ding Junwenyuan, on behalf of Mr. Wang Rutang, proposed to send the national arts team to various places to perform, scheduled to meet in Italy on September 1st, and explained that many places had sent letters requesting performances, and the expenses would be borne by the inviters. Ambassador Cheng and Dean Dai both attached Qian and gave instructions in person. The national arts comrades were all happy to go to promote the national light. On the 18th, the General Association of European Students held an annual meeting in Salo. Dean Dai publicly banqueted all the athletes and students. Many Chinese and Western guests attended. There was Peking Opera that day, and the national arts team performed again. The association also made and presented medals as souvenirs. Two kinds of Tai Chi exercise publications, in addition to being distributed to foreign guests during past performances, the rest were kept by the embassy and forwarded to libraries and foreign guests in various countries. The national arts team has two sets of weapons. The new ones were kept by Ambassador Cheng for display in the embassy, and the Tai Chi balls were planned by the angel to be transferred to the German Sports Hall. The sports film was also kept by the embassy for screening. Tai Chi exercises are novel in theory, and people from various countries come to ask for publications every day, which shows that foreigners are gradually understanding national arts. The national arts team left the German military camp on the 20th and will go to other places to perform. The commander of the German military camp also held a farewell banquet and sent off the team with a band upon departure, which was very touching. (Omitted below)

Shen Siliang Scheduled to Give Public Lecture 169

Mr. Shen Siliang, the executive director of the National Sports Promotion Association, returned home ahead of schedule on the 5th of this month. This decision to observe the World Games, where elites gathered, his experience should be more than that of others. The Youth Association on Sichuan Road in this city, in view of the backwardness of our country's sports, should learn from others. Under the guidance of the sports department, Mr. Peng Sanmei contacted Mr. Shen to give a public lecture. Mr. Shen has agreed and scheduled to give a public lecture on the 16th of this month (Wednesday) from 5:30 PM to 6:30 PM in the auditorium of the Youth Association on Sichuan Road. The topic has been set as "This World Games and China". At that time, Mr. Shen will analyze the reasons for our country's failure in the World Games and the experience we have gained in the World Games. The Youth Association believes that this lecture is closely related to the health of the nation and predicts that the listeners will be crowded. A special edition of 1,000 audience tickets will be issued, which can be requested from the association starting today and will be given away until they are gone. No exceptions will be made.

Women's Backstroke – New World Record 170

Havas News Agency, Copenhagen, 8th – At the 11th Olympic Games, the Dutch athlete Miss Senff won the women's 100-meter backstroke championship. She has now set a new world record for the women's 100-meter backstroke here, with a time of 1 minute 15.7 seconds, breaking the world record of 1 minute 18.2 seconds held by Miss Holm of the United States, and Miss Senff's own recent Olympic record of 1 minute 18.9 seconds.

Our Country's Athlete Delegation – Accompanying Expedition Diary (12th Letter) Special Correspondent Feng Youzhen from Central News Agency 176

Men's 400-meter Relay Preliminary Round

Held at 3:00 PM, the men's 400-meter relay preliminary round. 18 countries participated, divided into three groups. The top two from each group advance. The United States team, with a strong determination to win, fielded their most elite lineup. All three major generals participating in the 100-meter event appeared on the field, unchallenged. They equaled the world record with a time of 40 seconds flat. Our country was in the second group, with Chuan Yu Cheng running the first leg, Dai Shuguo the second leg, Cheng Jinguan the third leg, and Liu Changchun the final leg. They finished with a time of 44.8 seconds, trailing the first-place team by more than 20 meters. The results of each group are as follows:

First Group

1st United States (Owens, Metcalfe, Draper, Wykoff), 40 seconds (equals world record)

2nd Italy (Mariani, Cerri, Negri, Gonnelli), 41.1 seconds

Eliminated: Poofy 41.7 seconds, Finland 42 seconds

Second Group

1st Netherlands (Osendarp, Berger, Le Fleur, Broerse), 41.3 seconds

2nd Argentina (Liffner, Sandwaths, Houtmann, Spivak), 41.9 seconds

Eliminated: Hungary 42 seconds, Great Britain 42.4 seconds, France 42.6 seconds, China 44.8 seconds

Third Group

1st Germany (Litschom, Bormann, Gärmer, Hemberger), 41.4 seconds

2nd Canada ( Richardson, Hamber, Earle, McFee), 41.5 seconds

Eliminated: Sweden 41.5 seconds, Switzerland 42.2 seconds

Women's 400-meter Relay Preliminary Round

The women's 400-meter relay, originally with 14 participating countries, was divided into two preliminary groups. The top three from each group advance. France in the first group and Czechoslovakia in the second group did not run, so each group had only four countries starting. The results are as follows:

First Group

1st United States (Brandt, Rogers, Robinson, Vreeland), 47.1 seconds

2nd Canada (Brockshaw, Meagher, Van Malleon, Dawson), 48 seconds

3rd Netherlands (De Vries, Koning, Filles, Koolen), 48.4 seconds

Eliminated: Austria 49.9 seconds

Second Group

1st Germany (Albus, Krauss, Dollinger, Dörffeldt), 46.4 seconds, New Olympic Record

2nd Great Britain (Hisock, Ourney, Byming, Hook), 47.5 seconds

3rd Italy (Bogmanni, Ferra, Babarecco, Tistrina), 48.6 seconds

Eliminated: Finland 49.5 seconds

3000-meter Steeplechase Final

The 3000-meter steeplechase final was held at 4:00 PM. It was again a world for Finnish long-distance runners, with the three finalists finishing in 1st, 2nd, and 4th places. German athlete Dempert, who had the best time in the preliminary rounds, still defeated Mäntyranta to take third place. The results of the six finalists all broke the Olympic record (9 minutes 21.8 seconds, set by Lovkaka of Finland in 1928), and the first-place time shortened the Olympic record by as much as 18 seconds, which is truly remarkable.

1st Iso-Hollo (Finland) 9 minutes 3.8 seconds (all six broke Olympic Record)

2nd Toivonen (Finland) 9 minutes 6.8 seconds

3rd Dempert (Germany) 9 minutes 7.2 seconds

4th Mattilainen (Finland) 9 minutes 9 seconds

5th Manning (USA) 9 minutes 11.2 seconds

6th Larsson (Sweden) 9 minutes 16.6 seconds

1600-meter Relay Preliminary Round

The 1600-meter relay, with 17 participating countries, was held at 6:30 PM, divided into three preliminary groups. The top two from each group advance. The results are as follows:

First Group

1st United States (Cagle, Young, O'Brien, Fetz), 3 minutes 13 seconds

2nd Hungary 3 minutes 17 seconds, Eliminated: Poland 3 minutes 17.6 seconds, Japan 3 minutes 18.4 seconds

Second Group

1st Great Britain (Wolfe, Rampling, Powell, Brown) 3 minutes 14.4 seconds

2nd Sweden 3 minutes 14.6 seconds, Eliminated: France 3 minutes 15.2 seconds

Third Group

1st Germany (Hamming, Kinderpanag, Fölger, Harbig) 3 minutes 15 seconds

2nd Canada (Lyman, Edwards, Phipps, Loughlin) 3 minutes 15 seconds

Eliminated: Italy 3 minutes 16.6 seconds, South Africa 3 minutes 17.8 seconds, Czechoslovakia 3 minutes 22 seconds

Swimming

The swimming pool is built next to the main venue, extremely magnificent, accommodating more than 100 people. The eighth day of the Games saw the track and field events coming to a close, and swimming began. The spectators were more crowded than in the main venue. The first day of events included the men's 100-meter freestyle preliminary rounds and the women's 200-meter breaststroke preliminary rounds in the morning, and the men's 100-meter freestyle semi-finals and the women's 100-meter freestyle preliminary rounds in the afternoon. The results were excellent, and almost all existing tournament records were shattered. Among the participating countries, Japan showed the most impressive momentum, with a strong possibility of ascending to the throne of swimming. The United States experienced a significant decline, and it seems unlikely that they will be able to reclaim their titles at this Games. The results of each event are as follows:

Men's 100-meter Freestyle Preliminary and Semi-Final Rounds At 9:00 AM, swimming began with the first event, the men's 100-meter freestyle preliminary rounds. There were seven groups, with eight participants in the first two groups and seven participants in the remaining groups. The top two from each group and the two fastest third-place finishers from all groups advanced to the semi-finals. Our country's athlete Chen Zhenxing, although finishing fourth in the first group, was only about seven or eight meters behind. The best time among all groups was achieved by Japan's Taguchi Masaharu in the fifth group, with 57.5 seconds, breaking the tournament record (58 seconds set by Japan's Miyazaki Koji at the previous Games). The times of 57.7 seconds by the United States' Fick in the first group, 57.8 seconds by Japan's Yusa Masanori in the second group, 57.7 seconds by Japan's Arai Shigeo in the fourth group, and 57.9 seconds by Germany's Fissell were all below the Olympic record. The three participating athletes from Japan not only led the field but also achieved excellent results, displaying formidable strength.

First Group 1st Fick (USA) 57.7 seconds, New Olympic Record, 2nd Csik (Hungary) 58.3 seconds

Second Group 1st Yusa Masanori (Japan) 57.8 seconds, New Olympic Record, 2nd Hollander (USA) 59.9 seconds

Third Group 1st Ferec (GBR) 1 minute 0.7 seconds, 2nd Adjaluddin (Philippines) 1 minute 1 second

Fourth Group 1st Arai Shigeo (Japan) 57.7 seconds, New Olympic Record, 2nd Fissell (Germany) 57.9 seconds, New Olympic Record

Fifth Group 1st Taguchi Masaharu (Japan) 57.5 seconds, New Olympic Record, 2nd Christesen (Denmark) 1 minute 1.5 seconds

Sixth Group 1st Vvalfin (Yugoslavia) 1 minute 0.6 seconds, 2nd Haberl (Germany) 1 minute 1.4 seconds

Finance – HSBC Shilling Drops Below Statutory Level – Call Money Briefly Surges – Banks Forcefully Stem the Tide and Gradually Stabilize – Result: Rebounds by $1.80 177

The gold market initially weakened due to pure gold downstream yesterday. Surprisingly, the market suddenly became sluggish. Unexpectedly, HSBC's shilling listing declined, stimulating buying interest and a sharp rise in prices. Fortunately, banks forcefully stemmed the tide and gradually stabilized the situation. In the early morning, overseas silver markets saw the British market rise and the American market remain flat. Some market commentators claimed that after the market closed, there were only a few buyers below 0.0625, and that the market would be weak at the close. Montevideo forward silver prices rose by 2%. Exchange rates all showed an increase. London spot gold plummeted by 3 pence. The Central Bank's official exchange rate announcement revealed a half-and-half split between the British and American currencies. The customs gold unit fell by 4%. The standard call money price listing fell to $1,121.20. Off-market forward trading opened lower at $23.78. Although Hengyu advanced to over $4, Chunyuan, Yongyuan, Mao, Yongda, and Decheng liquidated their holdings. The morning opened with a low trading level, but quickly stabilized, as large investors took the opportunity to buy low. However, the market was still struggling. When HSBC's exchange rate listing was announced, the British currency shrank by 1.25, while the American currency rose by 1.25. The British exchange rate had decreased to 1 shilling, 2 and 25/100 pence. People's confidence in the Central Bank's ability to maintain foreign exchange rates suddenly experienced a degree of fear. This stimulated buying demand. Buyers rushed to buy, one after another, causing a gradual increase in prices. The banks were forced to sell foreign exchange to counter the buying and sellers were active at higher prices. A storm gradually subsided, but the market still struggled. The market conditions for the first half of the day are recorded below:

The morning opened at $1,123.90, a decrease of $1.30 from the previous closing price. Fuxingyong, Hengyu, Yuanmao, Yonghui, Xiangfu, Danda Natiao rose from $3.80 to $4.70. Chengda liquidated their holdings, retreating to $4.40. HSBC's listing revealed that the British currency shrank while the American currency rose by 1.25. Market sentiment quickly turned bullish. Huixiang, Yuanmao, Yongheng, Yufu, Taiyong, Fuxingyong, Yongnatiao immediately rose to $7.70. Chengda, Chunyuan, Qiafeng, Yongda, and Decheng sold off, falling to $6.00. Dadecheng, Dada, Heng, Yuanmao, Yongfuxingyong, and Hengyu still competed to buy, further rising to $9.50. Banks eagerly supplied foreign exchange. Chunyuan, Yongqiafeng, Yongfuxingyong took advantage of high prices, falling to $7.50. Dadecheng, Hengyu, Hengchangyong re-entered, rising to $8.40. Shenkang, Hengyu, and Chunyuanyong sold again, retreating to $7.20. Dahengfuxingyong took the opportunity to buy at low prices, rising back to $8.10. Shenkang advanced and emerged again. Dadecheng Yuanmaoyong also sold, with speculative downward pressure falling to $6.40. Retail investors and Qiafengyong repurchased, rising back to $7.11. After fluctuating, the market closed at $1,127 at noon. The post-closing market was still flat.

The closing price was based on the Central Bank's standard call money price, with the listing falling to $1,121.20. The theoretical pressure was weak at $6. For this month, the registered price was $1,124. For October, the price was $1,127. The morning replenishment water was $1,124. Pure gold was $1,131.90. The spot market was stable. Tianjin goods were priced at an additional $13.50. Cooked gold selling price was $15, buying price was $12, but there were no transactions.

The trading floor suddenly became chaotic. Fuxingyong, Futaiyong, Daheng, Dachang, Xianghong, Kangyong, Wanxing, Fuyu, Dadecheng, Xianghe Shen, Da Yongfu, Da Hengchangyong, Xiangfeng, Dafeng, Hengtong, Taichang, Hengyu, Huixiang, Tianfa Yuanmao Yong were on the buying side. Yuanmaoyong Huixiang bought in the beginning and then sold.

Checking the market conditions for the first half of the day, the market was initially weak but then became bullish. The morning opened at $1,123.90, with a high of $1,129.50, a low of $1,123.80. The market closed at $1,127 at noon. There were $5.70 ups and downs. The final result was a rebound of $1.80 from the previous closing price. Shilling Tightens and US Dollar Exchange Rate – Industry and Outside Participants Both Engaging in Speculation 178

The foreign exchange market experienced a surge and tightening yesterday due to HSBC's shilling listing. In the early morning, overseas cables reported that London large contracts rose by .0625 in both near and far terms. Market commentators claimed that there were a few buyers below the official listing price of .0625 after the market closed, indicating that the market would be sluggish at the close. New York silver markets remained unchanged. Montevideo forward silver prices rose by 2%. The British currency was worth 1.375 more against the US dollar, while the US dollar was worth 2.0625 more against the British pound. The British pound rose by 19 pound notes against the French franc, while the US dollar rose by 1.25 against the French franc. London spot gold plummeted by 3 pence. The Central Bank's official exchange rate announcement revealed that the British and American currencies were both flat. The customs gold unit fell by 4%. The foreign exchange market morning opening selling price in the near term was 1 shilling, 2 pence and 375/1000. The US dollar exchange rate was $30.25, indicating that the British currency tightened while the American currency loosened compared to the previous closing. The market was relatively flat after opening, with banks mostly engaging in offsetting transactions. When HSBC's listing was announced, the British currency shrank by 1.25, while the American currency rose by 1.25. The British currency listing had shrunk to 1 shilling, 2 pence and 25/100. Market sentiment suddenly turned bullish. The gold market suddenly rose. Chinese merchants were engaging in speculation one after another. The white silver balance tax also rose by 0.25. As the process gradually softened, the banks sold off while the currency was expensive. There were offsetting transactions from time to time, and the momentum gradually eased. At noon, the selling price for the near term was 1 shilling, 2 pence and 34375/1000. The US dollar exchange rate was $30.1875, indicating that both the British and American currencies tightened slightly compared to the previous close, due to exchange rate hedging. For the deferred term, the British currency was flat while the American currency tightened by 0.0625. Industry participants and outside participants such as yarn and flower shops were engaging in speculation. Day traders were also involved. HSBC's effort to stem the tide was relatively strong. The first half-day transaction record is recorded below:

The British exchange rate morning opening selling price in the near term was 1 shilling, 2 pence and 375/1000. Zhengjin Huabi sold to Oriental Mitsui for the October rate of 34375/1000. In the previous day's report, Da Feng Shuang entered 17,1910 packages, priced at 670 yuan, which was a duplicate of the report on the 5th. Furthermore, according to a letter from Da Feng Foreign Firm, "On the 6th, your newspaper published that our firm purchased 30 packages of grade B, 20-22 stripe fabric, priced at 615 yuan, and 10 packages of grade 5, 13-15 stripe fabric, priced at 655 yuan. Upon investigation, our firm did not purchase the above items on that day. The news is inaccurate. We request you to make a correction on our behalf. Thank you."

Editor's Note: This newspaper, recognizing that the information reported is difficult to ascertain accurately, thereby failing to meet the expectations of the readers, is striving to reorganize, aiming for more reliable and trustworthy news to provide readers with reference. However, silk market transactions are scattered, and information on market conditions and quantities is kept secret. Even well-informed correspondents sometimes find it difficult to know everything. The difficulty of this undertaking is evident. This newspaper is aware of the difficulty but still strives diligently to achieve it. The silk market conditions reported over the years, while not entirely satisfactory, are generally known to the readers. Fearing that there might be omissions, we sometimes use two reports to avoid being insufficiently detailed, preferring to err on the side of excess rather than deficiency. In the future, we still hope that people in the silk industry will provide assistance at any time to help achieve the purpose of this newspaper. Thank you very much.

Popular Lectures

Gauze Flowers. 180

After the Second Estimate of American Cotton Sharply Decreased, Standard Cotton Soars by One Dollar. Heavy Rain All Day Makes People Feel More Active. 181

Cotton Market Soars: Due to the Second Estimate Report of American Cotton, which showed a sharper-than-expected decrease, it soared by 51 to 63 points per pound. Osaka's Three Grades of Cotton rose by one dollar and fifty-six cents to over two dollars. Consequently, the market was shaken. At the same time, the weather was adverse, with continuous rainfall. Currently, cotton is in the boll-opening stage, which has a significant impact, making people feel more active and boosting buying interest. All months rose by eighty cents to one dollar.

Forward Contracts Break the Forty Dollar Barrier

The forward cotton market opened due to the publication of the American cotton second estimate report, which reported a volume of 11,121,000 bales, a sharp decrease of 1,360,000 bales compared to the previous estimate, rising 51 to 63 points per pound. Osaka's Three Grades of Cotton rose by over two dollars. As a result, the market was shaken, short sellers painfully closed their positions, and bulls increased their bets. Both sides advanced side by side, pushing market prices soaring. Furthermore, following the White Dew solar term, there was heavy rainfall, raising deep concerns about prolonged rain. Therefore, buying momentum increased. Hengyi, Zhenda, Gengfeng, Shenji, Yichang, and Fukang, all short sellers, uniformly resisted the advance, and forward months have already broken through the forty-dollar barrier. However, Yikang, Changfeng, Tongji, Mingde, Dachangcheng, and Meiji, all bulls, also unloaded a significant amount. As a result, all months rose by one dollar and twelve cents compared to the previous day's closing price. In the afternoon, trading opened with even heavier rainfall, and buying frenzy was unusually intense, but foreign merchants continued to sell, slightly stabilizing the market. Forced to retreat to Sanmu's prices, which caused a pullback. As a result, all months fell by twelve cents to thirty cents compared to the morning's closing price. Upon investigation, Changfeng sold 17,100 dan, Changhe 4,100 dan, Dachangcheng 4,300 dan, Yuanyi 4,900 dan, Mingde 6,100 dan, Tongji 3,400 dan, Meiji 2,300 dan, Shengyuan 2,000 dan, Yikang 15,100 dan, Yongchang 2,500 dan, Renfeng 3,200 dan, Taichang 1,700 zu, Juxing 2,000 dan, Tongfeng 2,000 dan, and Yicheng 2,500 dan. Shenji bought 15,700 dan, Yichang 7,200 dan, Fukang 5,400 dan, Yuanxingchang 3,000 dan, Tonghe 2,400 dan, Yongda 2,300 dan, Gengfeng 7,100 dan, Zhenda 3,400 dan, Xincheng 6,300 dan, Senkang 5,000 dan, Dachang 3,300 dan, Daji 5,000 dan, and Yukang 2,700 dan.

Fewer Spot Cotton Transactions

Spot cotton consumption has slowed down because futures cotton is rising, making negotiations difficult to reach an agreement, resulting in no transactions. The source, Yao cotton, has 500 bales, it is said.

Short Sellers Rush to Cover, Cotton Yarn Prices Rise Sharply, Following Raw Cotton's Advance. All Months Break the Two Hundred Dollar Barrier. 182

The yarn market is strong, with a sharp upward trend. Overseas yarn prices are soaring, and yarn sales have been brisk for days. People's sentiment is inherently stable. With the help of this positive news, market prices are advancing rapidly. At the same time, raw cotton is rising, making the yarn market even more robust. All months have broken through the two hundred dollar barrier.

One Chicken Jump Exceeds Three Dollars

The forward yarn market opened, and due to the reduction in American cotton production, buying interest in the market was strong. Short sellers were eager to cover their positions, and all months rose in a straight line, breaking through the two hundred dollar barrier. Three-grade yarn also rose by more than three dollars. As a result, the market was filled with buying orders, and the situation was tense. Yuda, Jinchang, Mingde, Changfeng, Dachang, and Tonghe all sold off, while Hengyi, Zhenda, Shenji Xincheng, Yongda, and Fukang bought heavily. As a result, all months rose by an average of three dollars and two to four cents compared to the previous day's closing price. Market transactions were exceptionally lively, and trading closed at 1:00 PM. In the afternoon, trading was extended to 3:00 PM, and the momentum remained strong. Because retail investors concentrated on covering short positions, all months rose by eight to nine cents to one dollar. Subsequently, profit-takers liquidated their positions, leading to a loosening and pullback. As a result, all months rose again by two, four, and five cents compared to the morning's closing price, while forward months fell by one, three cents. Upon investigation, Gengfeng sold 3,050 bales, Tonghe 3,000 bales, Dachang 2,400 bales, Changfeng 5,350 bales, Yuanyi 2,000 bales, Senkang 1,100 bales, Mingde 1,450 bales, Jinchang 3,500 bales, Yuda 2,750 bales, Tongji 1,600 bales, Meiji 1,500 bales, and Dafeng 1,100 bales. Dafu bought 1,000 bales, Hengfeng 6,100 bales, Zhenda 1,500 bales, Shenji 2,900 bales, Fukang 2,350 bales, Yongda 1,600 bales, Xincheng 7,700 bales, Senkang 1,900 bales, and Dachangcheng 1,000 bales. The highest and lowest prices of the day are listed on the left.

Estimated Quantity Sharply Reduced, American Cotton Surges by Over Sixty Points per Pound 183

Yesterday, American cotton opened, with all months up four to nine points per pound. The market situation was unstable in the early morning. Although prices were high, hedging sales increased. After the government estimate was released, the quantity was sharply reduced, and the public actively bought, causing prices to jump. Foreign merchants, Wall Street, and industry players all engaged in buying, and sentiment leaned towards long positions. Before the close, hedging sales and profit-taking caused some pullback, but demand remained good, and the close was firm. Spot prices rose by 63 points per pound, and futures prices rose by 51 to 63 points per pound. British spot cotton fell by seven points, and futures rose by 27 to 31 points. Indian cotton initially weakened due to long position liquidation and rain in the drought-stricken area, but then rebounded due to short covering. Pingle rose by half a rupee, and Omla rose, while Bailu Creek fell by 0.75 rupee. The original telegram is recorded on the left (8th day telegram).

According to a telegram from Mumbai, the opening prediction for the 9th was: Bailu Creek at 211 rupees, up 7.5 rupees; Omla at 197.5 rupees, up 5.25 rupees; Pingle at 161 rupees, up 4.25 rupees.

Three Grades of Yarn and Cotton also Rose Significantly On the 9th, a telegram from Osaka stated that Three Grades of futures yarn rose by one dollar and sixty cents to three dollars and thirty cents. The near month was 215.5 yuan, and the far month was 204.5 yuan. Futures cotton rose by one dollar and forty cents to two dollars and fifteen cents. The near month was 66.75 yuan, and the Da month was 64.7 yuan.

Piece Goods 185

Cotton Fabric Transactions are Increasingly Brisk. Japanese Merchants Open Over Three Hundred Pieces of Fine Twill for this Month. Guangdong and Guangxi Search for Local Factory's Fine Cloth and Fine Twill Very Eagerly. 186

Yesterday, cotton cloth was stimulated by the soaring domestic and foreign yarn and cotton prices. The market prices of all goods rose sharply, and industry sentiment was excellent. East goods fine cloth and fine twill rose by about one jiao per piece. Only ten-pound Dancing Cloth, 84 Flying Fish Dancing original cloth, sold at the original price due to weak demand. Japanese merchants still opened over three hundred pieces of fine twill for this month. Local factory goods fine cloth and fine twill, because Guangdong and Guangxi searched, all factories almost exhausted the current and future piece quantities, and the market price rose the most sharply, adding one jiao per piece. Fine cloth, coarse cloth, Tianjin, Guangdong, and Hankou guilds all purchased various brands, and the market price rose slightly. Yesterday, the Tianjin guild continued to purchase over four hundred pieces of sixteen-pound eleven-pound coarse cloth and twelve-pound coarse twill, and the market price has slightly increased by five fen per piece. Domestic and foreign factory serge and straight tribute merchants gradually increased prices. Four Gentlemen serge has now risen to two jiao and six fen per yard, straight tribute two jiao and seven fen, and Xuxian Village straight tribute satin two jiao and six fen, also because yarn and thread are soaring and products are lacking. After the Tianjin and Guangdong guilds poured in, Sichuan, the Yangtze River, Shandong, and local streets also competed to purchase, causing white goods and patterned goods to be in short supply and prices firm, and transactions were very brisk. Yihua Factory coarse cloth and coarse twill also sold over five hundred bags, it is said.

Grain 187

The Main Reasons for Expensive Flour (1) Foreign Wheat Continues to Rise (2) Cotton Yarn Soars. Floating Short Positions Compete to Cover, Suddenly Rising Five Fen and Seventy-Five Points. 188

Yesterday, after the flour market opened in the morning, prices for all months suddenly showed a uniform increase because foreign wheat prices in Chicago increased by about one jiao, and Canada increased by four to five jiao. When prices opened, it was raining heavily, and because cotton yarn was soaring, and foreign wheat prices seemed to have been rising for three or four days, various factors made people's sentiment active. The current month had previously risen sharply, reaching a maximum of three yuan and one jiao, and forward months also rose by two or three fen. Afterwards, in each round, the current month fell by nearly fen due to long position liquidation, and forward months also largely fluctuated. Until additional long positions were pulled in from outside the industry, and retail short positions also competed to cover positions rapidly, the market then rose by two or three fen. This upward trend was partly driven by cotton yarn and partly due to the continuous rise in foreign wheat and floating short positions competing to cover, it is said.

The Wheat Market is also Encouraged by Sentiment. All Months Rise by Four, Five, and Six Fen. 189

Yesterday's futures wheat market, when it opened in the morning, all months showed increases because foreign wheat prices continued to rise by one jiao to four or five jiao. Market sentiment, due to seeing rain after the White Dew solar term, inevitably had more concerns, and foreign markets also changed. Therefore, buyers were enthusiastic, and prices were immediately raised by three to five fen. Afterwards, because the flour market was good, prices were raised another one or two fen. When trading opened in the afternoon, transactions were still smooth, but the market turned flat, falling back one or two fen compared to the morning. This upward trend was really encouraged by sentiment. It was not like the improvement in flour sales, which seemed to have a solid foundation. The spot wheat market, because the standard rebounded, all grades increased by two or three fen. Shandong wheat opened at four yuan, nine jiao, two fen; second grade at four yuan, nine jiao; Guzhen wheat at four yuan, nine jiao; second grade at four yuan, eight jiao, eight fen; Yaowan wheat at four yuan, eight jiao, seven fen, and Jue eight jiao; Huai'an wheat at four yuan, seven jiao, three fen, and Jue six jiao and a half; Gaoyou wheat at four yuan, seven jiao and a half, and Jue seven jiao and three fen; Jiangbei wheat at four yuan, seven jiao, three or four fen; Bengbu wheat at four yuan, eight jiao, three fen, and Jue eight jiao; Wuhu wheat at four yuan, seven jiao, and Jue six jiao; Zhuzhen wheat at four yuan, seven jiao, eight fen, and Jue seven jiao and a half; Bao'ying wheat at four yuan, seven jiao, three fen; Hankou wheat at four yuan, five jiao and a half; Hunan wheat at four yuan, five jiao, seven fen; and Nanjing wheat at four yuan, seven jiao. Fuxin took 10,000 bags, Fufeng took 3,000 bags, and Shenda took 1,000 bags, it is said.

Chong'er's Perseverance and Determination 194

— Su Xi

During the Spring and Autumn period in our country, there was a prince of the State of Jin named Chong'er. From a young age, he had great ambitions and a fervent patriotic heart. Although he experienced various hardships and unbearable humiliations, in the end, he was able to respect the emperor and achieve hegemonic success, firstly because he had the help of wise and capable talents, and secondly because he himself had profound thoughts and a resolute will. There are many twists and turns in this story. Let's slowly tell it.

Initially, Chong'er's father, Duke Xian of Jin, was seduced by his favorite concubine and scared their three brothers away. Later, after Duke Xian died, the people of Jin welcomed Chong'er's younger brother, Yiwu, back and made him the ruler of Jin. This was called Duke Hui.

Chong'er was naturally Duke Hui's elder brother. When he was young, he wanted to be the leader of the hegemons. He often said to himself:

"When I grow up, I will definitely become a leader and make the lords of all directions obey my orders."

Not only did he have this great ambition, but he also had extremely intelligent and capable people to help him. Fox Yan, Jiu Fan, Zhao Cui, Xian Zhen, and Jia Tuo were all his right-hand men.

Cherishing great ambitions in his heart, he left his country and first fled to Pu City. His father, Duke Xian, secretly sent people to Pu City, wanting to kill him and the virtuous men who were helping him to eliminate future troubles. They received this news and fled together to the Di state.

When Chong'er arrived in the Di state, it so happened that the Di state had a very virtuous woman. The Di ruler married her to Chong'er. Although the couple lived a very happy life, his ambition to be a leader was still not forgotten. He often said to her:

"I not only want to be the ruler of Jin, but I also want to be the leader of the hegemons, so that the lords of all directions will listen to me. How happy would that be!"

After hearing these words, she encouraged him, saying:

"A true man should be like that!"

Chong'er fled to the Di state, but it was only to recuperate. Now that he had recuperated enough, and fearing that Duke Hui would send people to harm him, he decided to travel to various powerful states to broaden his knowledge and then find a way to return to his country. He said to Zhao Cui:

"Duke Huan of Qi is a very virtuous man. Let's go to his place."

When they were about to leave, the couple could not bear to part. Chong'er said to his wife:

"I want to be the leader of the hegemons within twenty-five years. If I can't do it, you should marry someone else."

His wife said:

"After twenty-five years, my hair will also be white. How can I still get married? I am determined to wait for you. Please concentrate on creating a great career and wish you success soon!"

Chong'er left the Di state and passed through the State of Wei. Duke Wen treated him very coldly. Along the way, when he passed Wu Lu, he was so hungry that his legs were weak and he could not move. He asked a peasant for food. The peasant also looked down on him and threw the food on a clay vessel. Chong'er was very angry at such humiliation and wanted to kill the rude peasant immediately. Zhao Cui persuaded him from the side:

"This is a sign of your future success. The clay vessel represents that you will definitely have a large territory in the future. Why are you angry?"

Chong'er listened to his words and was no longer angry. He accepted the food, thanked the peasant, and slowly went to the State of Qi. When he arrived in the State of Qi, Duke Huan treated him very well and married his clan daughter to Chong'er. Later, he lived in the State of Qi for more than two years, enjoying a very happy life. He even gradually forgot about his desire to return to his country and to become a hegemon.

Zhao Cui and others knew that if this continued for a long time, Chong'er's great ambition and great career would definitely disappear without a trace. They often discussed ways to get him to leave the State of Qi. One day, their conversation was overheard by the Qi woman, who advised her husband, Chong'er:

"You are the prince of Jin and bear a heavy responsibility. You should find a way to return to Jin. A man's ambition should be high. You must not let your lofty ambition disappear just for a woman. Moreover, there are these intelligent and hardworking virtuous men who are following you. How can you ignore them and be worthy of them?"

The Qi woman persuaded him earnestly several times, but Chong'er still did not listen. The Qi woman had no choice but to discuss with Zhao Cui and others. They first got him drunk with wine and then put him on a carriage and set off. Zhao Cui secretly thought that such a woman (referring to the Qi woman) did not do selfish things and could persuade Chong'er, clearly understanding the righteous path. It was truly admirable. He could not help but thank the Qi woman.

A few days later, Chong'er had already boarded the carriage in a drunken state and was sent out of the State of Qi by others. Not far away, he woke up, feeling very unwilling, and wanted to punish Jiu Fan. Jiu Fan knew what he meant and advised:

"My wish is to see you succeed in great things. Kill me, blame me, I am not afraid."

Chong'er's anger did not subside, and he said hatefully:

"If I fail to achieve success in the future, I will definitely eat your flesh."

Jiu Fan listened and replied very bravely and loyally:

"If you unfortunately fail in the future, then I will definitely be at the end of my wits and strength and will have died long ago, and my flesh will have rotted. How can you still eat it?"

When Chong'er heard these words, he suddenly woke up and felt very ashamed. He silently continued on his way. They first went to the State of Cao, where Duke Gong treated him very coldly. Then they went to the State of Song, where Duke Xiang welcomed him warmly. Chong'er saw that the State of Song had a strong army and wanted to borrow this army to return to his country. Later, he listened to Jiu Fan's advice and gave up the idea. Moving forward again, they went to the State of Zheng, where Duke Wen also treated him coldly. Zheng Shuzhan had already determined that Chong'er was a very talented and ambitious person. Fearing that he would cause trouble for the State of Zheng in the future, he advised Duke Wen to kill him at this time. Fortunately, Duke Wen did not listen to his words. However, Chong'er was already in extreme danger. Later, they fled to the State of Chu, where King Cheng treated him very well. One day, when they were having a banquet, they drank too much wine. The King of Chu said to Chong'er:

"If you can become the ruler of Jin in the future, how will you repay me?"

Chong'er stroked the hilt of his sword and smiled:

"There are many precious things. I will definitely not take them again. Perhaps when we fight in the future, I will definitely let you have ninety li of land."

At that time, the Chu general, Ziyu, was very angry and asked the King of Chu to kill him. The King of Chu knew very well that Chong'er was a talented person and that he had many wise people to help him. Such a person who could endure hardship and had perseverance could not be killed. Therefore, he did not kill him. But Chong'er went through another great crisis.

Later, when he went to the State of Qin, it so happened that Duke Hui of Jin died, and the State of Jin sent people to the State of Qin to welcome him. The State of Qin also sent people to escort him back to his country to become the ruler of Jin. This was called Duke Wen of Jin. At that time, he was already an old man with gray hair. But he was unwilling to be discouraged because of his old age and still wanted to pursue his hegemonic career.

In the fourth year of Duke Wen, the lords of various states joined forces with the State of Chu to bully the State of Song. Song asked Jin for help. Chong'er felt that the State of Chu had treated him well before, so he was now embarrassed to make things difficult for them. However, Song was a small country, and these weak nations had to be helped. So he was in a dilemma. Later, he listened to Fox Yan's words and learned that the State of Chu had just defeated the State of Cao and had close ties with the State of Wei. He used a strategy to attack Cao and Wei first. As expected, the State of Chu moved its troops to save Cao and Wei, and the siege of the State of Song was lifted. Later, the State of Chu attacked Song again, and Song again asked Jin for help. Chong'er was forced to fight the Chu army. At the beginning of the battle, he ordered his soldiers to retreat ninety li first, which was to fulfill the promise he had made to the King of Chu when he was in the State of Chu. As a result, the Chu army was defeated. Chong'er presented the many Chu soldiers he had captured to the Zhou Emperor and said respectfully:

"The State of Chu cannot respect the emperor's will and disrupts the lords of various states, relying on the power of a strong country to bully the small nations. We relied on justice to defeat them. Now, we are willing to offer these prisoners to Your Majesty to show that we will always respect the emperor's will."

The Zhou Emperor was very happy when he heard Chong'er's words and rewarded him heavily. He respectfully bowed several times before daring to accept the rewards. From then on, Chong'er became the hegemon.

He experienced all kinds of hardships and humiliations in his life, but he was able to adhere to his principles, so he finally achieved his ambition of becoming a hegemon. In this way, Chong'er can be said to deserve the four words "perseverance and determination" without any shame.

Playwright George Bernard Shaw 195

— Li Xishi

In February of the 22nd year of the Republic of China (1933), George Bernard Shaw came to China, staying in Shanghai for only one day before going to Beiping (Beijing). His purpose in going to Beiping was to admire China's ancient relics and scenic spots. At that time, many Chinese writers and politicians went to inquire about Shaw's opinions on the Chinese people. Readers will surely remember that the situation in Beiping and Tianjin was as serious as it is now. However, Rehe was still under the jurisdiction of the central government. This nearly eighty-year-old, unusually healthy Shaw expressed the following opinion: "China is currently in a critical period of survival. I dare not offer any advice, but I only hope that the Chinese people can save themselves from this situation. Because if the Chinese people can truly unite and work together, I believe that no one in the world can resist them."

George Bernard Shaw was born in Dublin, Ireland, in 1856. His father was an elderly, retired minor official who was fond of drinking. This elderly drunkard, recognizing the bleak future and the heavy responsibility, took all of his future pension to start a bread business. However, the result was completely contrary to expectations. Not only did it fail to improve his living situation, but it also left him penniless. Shortly after this failure, he passed away from excessive grief and depression.

Fortunately, Shaw's mother was not as easily discouraged by setbacks as her husband was. She set her sights and struggled forward. Because she had a special interest in music, shortly after her husband's death, through diligent effort, she actually gained a considerable position in the Dublin music scene, relying on her daily income to support her orphaned children and herself. Shaw was fortunate to have such a talented mother, even in such circumstances. Later, she gained the highest support in the literary world, and we cannot ignore her mother's contributions.

When Shaw was studying in elementary school, he was a child who refused to be subdued by his environment. He studied very hard, but he opposed mindless rote learning. He saw many classmates holding textbooks all day long, tirelessly memorizing, reading wherever the teacher told them to, without considering whether they thoroughly understood the meaning of the text. Shaw was most opposed to this way of studying. In history class, when the teacher wanted him to memorize many historical dates and unimportant names and places, he resolutely refused. He felt that such studying not only did not help his knowledge, but also needlessly damaged his brain, which was too meaningless. He did not pay much attention to textbooks. If it was a subject that suited his temperament, he would put in extra effort, not releasing the book until he truly understood it. At the age of fifty-four, he graduated from a commercial school and then became a clerk at the Dublin Land Company. That year, two American missionaries came to Dublin to preach. Shaw, upon hearing this news, had his rebellious spirit aroused. He took a public letter and published it in the local newspaper. The main idea of this letter was to oppose superstition and to explain that there was no such thing as "God" in the world. When people with outdated ideas in the area saw this letter, they were very shocked and angry, saying that Shaw was a religious rebel.

When Shaw was twenty years old, his mother decided to go to London to make a living, and he had no choice but to follow her. Their move was indeed too dangerous because they did not know anyone in the vast city of London, and they had little money. However, this virtuous and promising mother was not afraid of these difficulties and fought hard in this society. Before long, she found a job that allowed her to support herself. At that time, Shaw worked hard reading literary books all day long. Undoubtedly, his lifelong determination to dedicate himself to literature was decided at that time. In the first three years in London, he worked as a bookkeeper in a store, but whenever he had the opportunity, he worked hard on literature. In his free time, he went to the library to read books or participated in various social activities because he had a very clear understanding of society. If you want to be a writer, but you are ignorant of the situation in society, then you will never write great works.

Although Shaw wrote many novels and submitted them to various places, they were all met with the cold eyes of the editors and were thrown into the wastepaper basket. However, he was not discouraged at all, but put more effort into literature.

When he recalled the situation of his manuscripts being rejected by the editors, he said, "Life is like war. If you cannot muster the courage to persevere to the end when you are fighting, then you will be defeated by it. If I had relaxed my hopes and determination because of temporary failures, then I would never have the position I have in the literary world today."

When he was twenty-six, the American socialist Henry George came to London to give lectures. Shaw, who was accustomed to participating in social activities, also attended. After listening to Henry's lecture, he was greatly moved. Two years later, he united several close friends who shared his ideas and organized a group to save and transform society. The members of this group were all famous scholars at the time. They witnessed the injustices of the world, so they wanted to transform society. Their idea was to gradually get mutually hostile people to find ways to connect and cooperate. Shaw did a lot of valuable things in this group, so he was not only a writer but also a social reformer. At that time, he did a lot of criticism. However, before the age of thirty-seven, he was still an ordinary person, and he still had no status in society as before. But in that same year he published a play, "Mrs. Warren's Profession", which caused a sensation in the entire European literary world. The major theaters in England competed to rehearse it. When it was staged, it was truly a sea of people, extremely crowded, and it received applause and cheers from the audience. From then on, George Bernard Shaw's fame in the literary world was established. After that, he wrote many plays, all of which were very famous. In 1926, he won the Nobel Prize in Literature. Since then, the world has recognized him as a great playwright. Yes, nothing is ever done in vain. If you put in effort, you will always have success. It was only because Shaw endured hardship and hardship that he has achieved today's success. This was not a lucky win but a well-deserved reward.

To Contributing Writers: I would like to wake you up, please consider your readers and the mission of this publication. This publication does not intend to cater to intellectuals or literary figures who are already well-educated, so the writing must be popular and clear. If you have a fresh and unique style, it is better to submit it elsewhere. In terms of style, we want stories, not news reports, and not missionary arguments. The topic should be new and interesting, but it should be written in a way that is understandable to the general public. Here is a method you might try: read the completed article aloud to illiterate people in your family and see if they can understand it and are interested. If the author has seen too many new things, he may wish to go back and look at texts such as "Stories Old and New" and "The Travels of Lao Ts'an". ——Editor

Publishing World

Jane Eyre: An Autobiography (Part 4) 196

— Chen Youqin

Written by English C. Brontë, translated by Li Jiyie, published by the World Literature Series of the Life Bookstore

As a result, Rochester committed bigamy and deceived the innocent and pure young girl, Jane Eyre. The circumstances forced Rochester to announce the truth: the madwoman living in the attic of Thornfield Hall was his legal wife. He had been deceived and involuntarily married Bertha Antoinetta Mason, who had not yet developed her madness. The person who had repeatedly tried to kill Rochester and had bitten her brother, Richard Mason, was none other than Rochester's legal wife, Mason. These were the great secrets of Thornfield Hall, all of which Jane Eyre had inexplicably experienced firsthand. A group of people, including Briggs, made a special trip to visit the beast-like madwoman, who fought with Rochester on the spot.

Bertha Antoinetta Mason's madness was hereditary. She also had a brother who was completely mute and an idiot. However, her father was a planter and wealthy merchant in the West Indies. Rochester's father and brother, in order to obtain the wealthy merchant's daughter's dowry of 30,000 pounds, facilitated this unfortunate marriage. At first, she was not crazy, but she became crazy after marrying Rochester. After going crazy, she was confined to the third floor of Thornfield for ten years. For a great price, a maid, Grace Poole, was hired to watch over her, and a doctor, Carter, was specially contracted to prevent temporary accidents.

Since this secret was revealed, Jane Eyre could not bear such a great shock and could not bear to see someone already having a wife while she willingly became someone's mistress, so she left.

Alone, she sleepily stole away from Thornfield Hall. It was just before dawn when she boarded a bus going to an unknown destination, paid the driver the only twenty shillings she had on her, and was taken to a very, very far intersection called Whitcross, where she got off the bus. She also lost the small package of clothes she had brought with her. Disoriented, she stumbled into a small town, wanting to find a small job, even wanting to find a servant's position, but she was rejected everywhere. Helpless, she could only beg and sleep in the open.

One rainy night, she approached a house in a village called Morton. She saw two young girls reading inside through the window. She knocked on the door to beg, but was rejected by an old woman. In the face of hunger and cold, she fainted at the door. When the male owner of the house returned from outside, he discovered this dying beggar girl. He called the women inside the house to rescue her. Fortunately, because of the soup feeding, she woke up, and the young girls gave her their warm bed. After resting for a few days, she was completely well.

The owner of the house was named St. John Rivers, and he was a pastor. He had two sisters, one named Mary and one named Diana, and an old maid named Hannah. They questioned her about her background. She kept her secret, changed her name to Jane Elliott, and only told them the history of Lowood School, hiding the events at Thornfield.

She lived with St. John's family in Morton for some time, and they got along very well with each other. She asked St. John to introduce her to a job so that she could live independently, even if it was as a seamstress, a nurse, or a servant. Later, St. John introduced her to be the headmistress of a cottage school in his parish, which she naturally took on with great pleasure. The funding for the school was provided by Mr. Oliver, the owner of the valley's needle factory and foundry. His only daughter, Miss Oliver, had also taught at the school, but now she did not have time, so she hired Jane Eyre. St. John and Miss Oliver already had considerable affection for each other, but St. John, who was dedicated to the church, did not think that the wealthy Miss Oliver was his ideal match.

St. John was going to accompany Hannah to do pastoral work. Diana and Mary were working as nannies in fashionable cities in southern England. Because of poverty, everyone had to go their separate ways, so the house in Morton had to be locked up. Although they all felt reluctant and had many sad expressions.

At the cottage school, she met Miss Oliver and became good friends. She did a sketch of Miss Oliver's beautiful face. This artistic talent surprised Miss Oliver. Soon, St. John also saw it when he came to the school.

Miss Oliver was very beautiful, and St. John was also very handsome. They were a match made in heaven, but unfortunately, because of the relationship between rich and poor classes, there was an invisible obstacle. Furthermore, St. John wanted to realize his sacred ideal career and go to India to preach. He felt that only Jane Eyre, who had insight, perseverance, and a sharp mind, was his only qualified assistant.

One night, late at night, St. John came. He revealed to Jane all of her past history (because he had received a letter from the lawyer Briggs) and told her that she was now a wealthy woman with a inheritance of 20,000 pounds. This inheritance was designated to her by her uncle, Mr. Eyre, in his dying will. Jane, in her surprise and joy, immediately suggested dividing the 20,000 pounds, with St. John, Diana, Mary, and herself each getting one-quarter—5,000 pounds.

As for why the lawyer Briggs wrote to St. John about the relationship with Jane's mother? It turned out that St. John's mother's surname was Eyre. She was Jane's father's sister. The big wine merchant, Mr. Eyre, was Jane's uncle, and also St. John's uncle. Eyre and St. John, Diana, and Mary were cousins. Everyone did not know each other, but met unintentionally.

The lawyer Briggs was Mr. Eyre's lawyer. He wrote to St. John saying that his uncle, Mr. Eyre, had died and left his property to his brother's orphaned daughter. A few weeks later, he wrote again, saying that the heiress was missing and asked St. John if he knew any news about her. He unintentionally discovered Jane's real name from a painting and a piece of paper. He then realized that "Elliott" was an assumed name.

After all of this truth was understood, the vacation season was approaching. She returned to Morton in advance, cleaned up and tidied up the old house, arranging it very properly, waiting for Diana and Mary to return, so everyone could enjoy this vacation. During the holidays, their happiness naturally increased a hundredfold compared to before because they were no longer paupers without anything.

History of Gonorrhea Treatment 197

— Dr. Yang Daonan, Graduate of the Russian Labor Medical University

The latest treatment was invented after research by many scholars and under government incentives

Before the invention of stimulation therapy, many scholars were racking their brains, burying themselves in books and laboratories. In the wards, there was initially the so-called transmembranous sterilization therapy for gonorrhea, which used drugs to clear the urethra and gradually reduce the gonorrhea bacteria on the urethral mucosa. This was very popular for a time. After disappointment, scholars encouraged each other with the saying "failure is the mother of success" and conducted more meticulous research.
